The Alchemy Workshop over there should have made quite a profit."

Chen Pingan said, "The two cross-ocean ferries from the Gold Armored Continent pooled a large sum of divine money to purchase that ascended corpse's head. To ensure a safe return with their treasures, they even paid a hefty sum to hire a sword immortal as escort."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child grumbled, "Those at the Alchemy Workshop are truly annoying. It's as if I'm stopping them from slaughtering these upper-level demons. Whether it's thousands or just a few, I have my hands full, and I gain no benefit from it. Why blame me? Is it that hard to understand such a simple principle? What a hassle."

Chen Pingan replied, "They don't blame you. Everyone empathizes, willingly respects their seniors, and sword cultivators don't look down on you because of your demon identity. How can you still survive? Can you even face yourself? There’s no need for you to overthink it. You should be secretly pleased."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child chuckled. "You're quite right, truly right. Unfortunately, I've heard too little of such straightforward reasoning in the past. That Ah Liang didn’t hit the nail on the head; he just deceived me into thinking that the ascended demons of the righteous world live like immortals, that founding a sect wouldn't be difficult."

As they walked, they finally encountered the first demon cultivator.

It was a great demon in the Immortal realm, coiled like a mountain, surrounded by miasma.

Chen Pingan approached the cage bars, focusing his gaze but still couldn't see clearly.

This prison held six upper-level demons, sixty-one mid-level demons, and at least three lower-level demons.

The dead would be thrown to the Alchemy Workshop, their bodies treasures to be fully utilized. Some managed to leave alive, either going to the Mirage or fighting among themselves or against sword cultivators. Additionally, Old Hearing-Impaired Child had picked out some disciples for training. If he taught them swordsmanship, anywhere outside this Sword Qi Great Wall, it would be a coveted opportunity. An ascended being teaching sword techniques would be something worth learning even in death.

The problem was that here, Old Hearing-Impaired Child's swordsmanship was too advanced. It was too easy for those learning to break through, but once they reached the Nascent Soul stage, they would die.

Many demons deliberately stagnated at the Golden Core stage, effectively burning themselves out. If their cultivation didn't rise, their lifespans would shorten, leading to death, either from shattered Dao hearts or being blown to bits by the ever-growing sword energy. As for the physical bodies, Old Hearing-Impaired Child would still use his methods to preserve them; otherwise, the Alchemy Workshop would hold him accountable.

About Old Hearing-Impaired Child's background, the Summer Retreat Palace had some records. It was quite strange; he was an ascended great demon who pretended to be a sword cultivator, having refined several sword immortals' relics into flying swords, similar to how Chen Pingan had refined his own as essential tools. Old Hearing-Impaired Child's cultivation was sufficiently high, and he possessed three refined flying swords, giving him an appearance more like that of a sword cultivator than an immortal.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child had once been a powerful demon in the wild world, but upon arriving at the Sword Qi Great Wall, he had settled into the role of a weary jailer, perhaps secretly thinking of "nurturing another flying sword of his own at the thirteenth stage."

As for the Immortal realm demon before Chen Pingan, it was quite legendary. Initially imprisoned at the Nascent Soul bottleneck, it unexpectedly broke through to the Immortal realm over a millennium in this oppressive place.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child asked, "Lord Hidden Official, shall we make our move now?"

The old man was curious why the young Hidden Official had not brought along that sword-immortal-grade divine weapon and intended to rely solely on his fists to kill an Immortal realm demon. It was hard to say who would exhaust whom. Of course, Old Hearing-Impaired Child knew that Chen Pingan possessed a unique fist technique that could accumulate power with each strike, which was quite formidable. However, as a body cultivator at the bottleneck of the Golden Body stage, his physique was still not resilient enough. To kill this Immortal realm demon, Chen Pingan would not last until his final punch. Faced with an Immortal realm being, the disparity in realms was too vast. Even if Cao Ci came, he would still be helpless.

If he were to seek help and then employ such techniques, he would lose all significance, making it not worthwhile.

Moreover, Old Hearing-Impaired Child felt that unless Chen Pingan was a ninth-stage martial artist, there might be some hope of enduring the pain of disintegration of body and soul. 

Even if the young Hidden Official's martial arts level was comparable to that of Cao Ci or Yu Juanfu, they could be viewed as having a higher realm, but even as a far-traveling martial artist, Chen Pingan still fell short of a full realm.

Chen Pingan began to move, "No rush."

He continued walking, glancing at things before moving on.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child couldn't help but ask, "Lord Hidden Official?"

Chen Pingan said, "We'll make a round first. At most, we’ll waste a trip back. It won't delay the main business."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child laughed and asked, "So this is just about that? Does it matter?"

Chen Pingan smiled. "Consider it a stroll."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child said, "A young person should be more flexible and resilient; it isn't good to be too rigid. While it’s easier to do things precisely and be ruthless with people, it can easily sap one's vitality and harm one's fortunes."

Chen Pingan smiled. "Senior, your insights are indeed wise words. Being overly cautious can lead to a small heart."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child, who had struggled in the Sword Qi Great Wall for three thousand years, was surprised to hear someone call him “senior” so many times and to engage in such lengthy conversation with a sword cultivator.

Chen Pingan asked, "How had the Grand Sword Immortal arranged matters with you before?"

Old Hearing-Impaired Child replied, "When I leave the city to fight with all my might, first, I’ll kill all the demons imprisoned here. Of course, that has changed to Lord Hidden Official doing it personally. Secondly, I can take three Golden Core disciples with me as exceptions."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child didn’t mention his years of cultivation in the wild world; he had endured for over three thousand years in the Sword Qi Great Wall.

After suffering for three thousand years, he was still only at the Immortal realm, without gaining the title of "Sword Immortal."

As they proceeded, they finally saw a fresh face—a demon cultivator curled up and lying down. Looking human, upon noticing Old Hearing-Impaired Child and Chen Pingan, he pretended not to see.

The few upper-level demons behind him, though suppressed, still emitted cold, wandering gazes that felt almost tangible. Some great demons appeared frantic, violently crashing against the sword light bars, bloodied but unwilling to stop. Eventually, they gripped the sword light tightly, cursing Old Hearing-Impaired Child and the unfamiliar young man, Chen Pingan. Chen Pingan stopped, and in the familiar tongue of the wild world, asked several questions, only to be met with incessant curses.

There were also those demons who bowed and begged for mercy, including a graceful fox spirit, still radiant at a thousand years of age, looking as delicate as a young girl. Upon seeing the young Hidden Official, she sat sideways, hand on her heart, biting her lip tightly, on the verge of tears. Others among the demons swore they would become slaves, just to leave this place alive. Chen Pingan remained silent throughout.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child smiled and said, "That fox spirit, even with only seven tails, wouldn’t be beneath you, Lord Hidden Official, if you took her in as a maid. I believe you still have that much authority, and there’s no need to worry about her loyalty."

Chen Pingan didn't respond.

He suddenly recalled the mountain cliff path he had traversed on a snowy night during his return home from the Great Sui years ago.

Over these years of travel, he had indeed encountered many fox spirits. However, he had never had the chance to visit the Fox Kingdom of the Xu family in Qingfeng City. Xu Yuanxia had once said that any man who had not visited the Fox Kingdom would never understand the tender beauty and the hero's grave.

Among the four ladies of the righteous world, one had a close relationship with Ah Liang, the Lady of the Azure Sacred Mountain in the Bamboo Sea Paradise. Then there was the elusive Lady of the Rosy Cheeks from the Central Divine Continent, who had exchanged a plum garden for a letter that would eventually reach the scholarly Chen Chun'an. She merely hoped that the South Posa Continent would treat this upper-level demoness with kindness. Ultimately, seeking a protective talisman from a Confucian saint for Lady Rosy Cheeks was also a long-term consideration for Lu Zhi. 

With a higher realm, one would face greater calamities. Lu Zhi was not the kind of sword immortal willing to act smoothly. Once she entered the South Posa Continent, she would be considered an outsider. Scholars consider many convolutions; they fear the overt schemes that leave Lu Zhi no choice but to draw her sword, which would be a great disaster. Thus, having Lady Rosy Cheeks supporting and strategizing for Lu Zhi was more reassuring. But Chen Pingan also worried that Lady Rosy Cheeks' heavy grievances might subtly influence Lu Zhi.

So, when Chen Chun'an intervened, it would be both protection and oversight, preventing Lady Rosy Cheeks from acting on impulse.

However, Lady Rosy Cheeks was likely unaware of this, still curious about the merit the young Hidden Official had promised. Chen Pingan had no intention of revealing anything in advance; everything would become clear once she accompanied Lu Zhi to the South Posa Continent.

Then there was a lady regarded as the most orthodox descendant of the Moon Palace, whose fate remained unknown. Chen Pingan had long confirmed that it was the Lady of the Gui family, a hidden patron.

Lastly, there was the nine-tailed celestial fox, Lady Huanxi, who had also vanished without a trace.

At the very bottom of the prison, the last cage resembled a watery cell, with water no more than two feet deep, covering about an acre, its deep emerald hue concentrated. It had manifested into numerous small green fish; the water was so clear that every detail was visible. Those suddenly motionless green fish seemed to float in the air. Inside, a young demon was poking his head out, his body below the water completely invisible, appearing as if he were merging with it.

It could be a method for nurturing dragons?

The demon youth's face bore faint scales, with slight protrusions resembling deer antlers on either side of his forehead.

Chen Pingan, hands tucked into his sleeves, stopped and locked eyes with the boy.

He was at the Cave Dwelling stage, having transformed into human form not long ago.

Ultimately, he excelled due to his exceptional talent. On the cultivation path, to earn the favor of the ancestor, one must first earn the favor of the heavens. Whether one can cultivate or not—

Chen Pingan began to head back, marveling, "If he gains the opportunity to practice swordsmanship and cultivate, with a mentor leading the way and further questioning the Dao heart, these three disciples of yours will be astonishingly successful."

Including the young boy, their current realms were Cave Dwelling, Dragon Gate, and the bottleneck of Golden Core.

This cage did not imprison strays or nobodies. The younger the demon cultivators, the more remarkable their innate talents.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child smiled bitterly. "Lord Hidden Official, surely not?"

This young man was indeed troublesome, but he could still be slapped dead with a casual hand.

The problem was that Chen Qingdu would have slapped himself dead before anyone else.

Chen Pingan could resolutely breach the contract and kill all three disciples without a second thought. Considering Chen Qingdu's temperament, would he show favoritism? Need one even think?

Chen Pingan said, "All along, senior, you have adhered to your principles, and I respect you deeply."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child scoffed. "But?"

Chen Pingan laughed. "Since you're so good at conversation, please continue. I am all ears."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child had no intention of making a deal with this young man.

He shouted loudly, "Grand Sword Immortal, is this acceptable? Aren't you going to intervene?"

No response.

Chen Pingan continued, "The three selected by you should all have upper-level potential, right?"

Old Hearing-Impaired Child nodded helplessly.

Chen Pingan said, "Then we can count one as Jade Pure, and two as Immortal realms, of course, as sword cultivators. I will request three opportunities for cultivation from you, whether it be techniques or treasures, preferably ones suited for demon cultivation."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child breathed a sigh of relief; these matters were merely trifles to an ascended cultivator. "Two Jade Pure realms and one Immortal realm. If luck is bad, it could be one Nascent Soul realm and two Jade Pure realms."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child wasn’t deceiving anyone.

A sword cultivator with upper-level potential and whether they ultimately become upper-level sword immortals were two different matters.

To speak of the living and not the dead—Yan Ming, Yin Chen, and Nalan Caihuan, who among them wasn't a gifted sword immortal candidate? And now, what had become of them?

Chen Pingan agreed. "I will listen to you, senior."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child laughed. "It seems that calling you 'senior' is not in vain."

Chen Pingan cupped his fists. "Please, senior, don’t hold a grudge."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child shook his head. "It’s not worth it."

Chen Pingan said, "This cage is, in fact, a divine corpse that has lost its head, isn't it?"

Old Hearing-Impaired Child nodded.

As they approached a cage Chen Pingan initially thought was empty, suddenly a figure stepped out from the mist barrier.

Chen Pingan turned to look; it was a woman with a pale face and bright red lips, appearing youthful. A stitched bag hung from her wrist.

From the neck down, her appearance was ghastly, unrecognizable, almost more ghostly than a ghost.

Her skin was devoid of flesh, almost transparent, with visible organs and veins writhing.

Chen Pingan, accustomed to bloody and bizarre sights, felt a shiver upon seeing this woman.

The Summer Retreat Palace had no records of her.

The woman approached the bars and took a step closer, almost face-to-face with Chen Pingan, who remained still.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child chuckled. "Her name is Nianxin; she’s a seamstress who ended up here during a great upheaval in the Gold Armored Continent."

Chen Pingan understood.

A seamstress.

Extremely rare.

Chen Pingan had once come across her in a secret archive dedicated to unorthodox practitioners in the Summer Retreat Palace.

While not ancient history, it was far too sinister and classified as demonic.

In the history of the righteous world, orthodox talisman cultivators would kill such a being on sight.

The four difficult spirits on the mountain: sword cultivators, Mo family debt collectors, Daoist priests from the sword house, and disciples of the Legalist school. However, these cultivators were merely troublesome; they were the most feared by practicing Qi cultivators, but they didn’t carry infamy. Beyond that, there were ten types of practitioners that could be considered public enemies, far worse than wild practitioners.

For instance, those who carried Dragon King's nets to capture exhausted serpents for their masters in the South Sea, although not high in rank, merely Earth Immortals, yet even sword immortals could not kill them, as they enjoyed stealing from the rivers.

Then there were those who specialized in refining graves, easily provoking the passage of ghost soldiers, termed as "passers."

And the woman before Chen Pingan was the legendary seamstress, proficient in talisman crafting, using human skin as talisman paper.

Her fundamental principle was "to make garments for others."

The secret records indicated that to practice this method, one must first skin themselves, enduring the pain of being flayed as the first step. The second step involved traversing a hell-like realm akin to Fengdu's ghost gates. Afterward, there were several more trials.

Chen Pingan had long found it puzzling what significance there was in choosing to practice such a method.

The woman took a step back, circling around Chen Pingan, and then halted to ask, "How old are you?"

Chen Pingan remained silent.

The woman, referred to as Nianxin by Old Hearing-Impaired Child, was not bothered; she continued, "That shouldn’t be an illusion. So you came from a prominent family in Tai Xiang Street? The family elders finally persuaded Chen Qingdu to help you establish a martial temple, gaining the fortune of the Sword Qi Great Wall?"

Chen Pingan shook his head. "I am an outsider; I practice my punches diligently."

The woman seemed a bit disappointed. "Chen Qingdu is still too cautious. He has many methods he is reluctant to use."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child, smirking, said, "You’re young and only have some flashy skills, so don’t call the Grand Sword Immortal by name."

Then he reminded the woman, "Nianxin, this is the new Hidden Official of the Sword Qi Great Wall."

The woman tilted her head, staring at Chen Pingan, and spoke intermittently, "Left-handed. Dragon. Rebuilt the Changsheng Bridge. Both body and soul severely stitched. Practiced martial arts first, then nurtured the flying sword. Your control over your body is meticulous, half a fellow practitioner. Strong killing intent, hmm, it has intensified now. But you can fully manage that killing intent; at your young age, that’s impressive. No wonder you’re the new Hidden Official."

Chen Pingan remained in place, smiling. "Miss Nianxin, you have a keen eye."

Old Hearing-Impaired Child knew Nianxin well, so he was not surprised by her methods.

The prison was strange, with free movement, and Nianxin was one of them.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child suddenly asked, "Why don’t you call him 'senior' and instead refer to him as 'mister'?"

Chen Pingan retorted, "Doesn’t senior drink without any snacks?"

Old Hearing-Impaired Child was taken aback.

In the distance, a childish voice piped up, "This guy is mocking you for loving to speak drunken nonsense and saying things that don’t fit the occasion."

Chen Pingan turned to look; it was a white-haired boy sitting cross-legged in mid-air, his forehead unusually large, with two green snakes adorning it and two short swords at his waist.

His eyes sparkled, and he was bored, gnawing on his fingers.

Old Hearing-Impaired Child shot a sidelong glance and explained to Chen Pingan, "He's an external celestial demon."

Chen Pingan nodded.

The white-haired boy said, "Old Hearing-Impaired Child, quickly call me grandpa!"

Old Hearing-Impaired Child complied, calling out "grandpa."

The white-haired boy scowled. "Why are you so unenergetic?"

The woman disregarded Old Hearing-Impaired Child and the boy, fixing her gaze on Chen Pingan, saying, "Can you really endure the pain? Don't die on me."

Chen Pingan smiled. "We'll see."

Then he felt a chilling sense of foreboding as the woman smiled seductively, gracefully performing a deep bow. "For the young master, I shall add layers against the cold, stitching by lantern light."

*(End of Chapter)*

 **Chapter 788: Life’s Dream Within a Dream**

Chen Ping'an was not startled by Nianxin’s shocking words, but rather by the intense and focused gaze of this seamstress, which made him quite uncomfortable. 

Was this the same kind of gaze he had when rummaging through the trash at the Baofu Studio, spotting treasures and wealth on the ground?

Nianxin said, "Wait until you reach the realm of Long-distance Travel (Yuan You) before we talk. I don’t want to help you collect your corpse."

As for whether this young Hidden Official could break through to a new realm and how, Nianxin didn’t care in the least.

Chen Ping'an nodded, already planning his course as he walked along.

Nianxin floated away, disappearing in an instant, clearly unbound by any constraints.

Chen Ping'an threw out three questions in one breath: "How old is Nianxin? What realm is she at? What is her foundation?"

The old deaf man chuckled but said nothing.

Chen Ping'an continued, "I can refrain from doing anything to that boy in the water prison."

The old deaf man laughed, "As a scholar, how can you be so careless?"

Chen Ping'an ignored him, crouching down and lightly tapping the road with his fingers, producing a sound like metal clashing. He then spread his palm over the ground.

Truly, this corpse of an ancient divine being was quite strange.

It was apparent that the old deaf man valued that boy the most and had the highest stakes in him. Of course, it was possible that there was some sleight of hand involved, but ultimately, only three demon races had survived, so the old deaf man’s tricks could only go so far.

Chen Ping'an carefully re-examined the secret files pertaining to the Summer Resort Palace in his mind. He found that the three individuals chosen by the old deaf man were quite obscure, and he could confirm that the previous Hidden Official, Xiao Xian, must have had some dealings with the old deaf man, which was why the Hidden Official lineage had concealed some crucial information. Chen Ping'an had no intention of digging up old grievances regarding these long-standing issues, and besides, he might not even be able to do so. With the old deaf man beside him, a transcendent being, it wouldn't be wise to provoke him. After all, the old deaf man was willing to save face for him primarily because of the Big Sword Immortal. Holding a Hidden Official jade token in his hand while being someone who was not even a sword immortal was of little use.

However, while this reasoning held, business could still be conducted. After all, Chen Ping'an and the old deaf man had no grudges against each other. If they were to tear their faces apart, the younger one with the greater official rank would inevitably gain the upper hand.

Thus, Chen Ping'an's approach to business was simple: he was straightforward in telling the old deaf man that training three disciples here was akin to raising tigers in Sword Qi Great Wall, but since this was at the behest of the Big Sword Immortal and could not be altered, allowing them to leave the prison right under my eyes as if letting a tiger return to the mountain could indeed be arranged. There were many ways for the three disciples to survive.

The agreement between you, the old deaf man, and the Big Sword Immortal, is not in conflict with the final decision of the Summer Resort Palace.

Perhaps the old deaf man had become accustomed to being manipulated in Sword Qi Great Wall, and although he had suffered a small loss, he had at least gained the promise of the young Hidden Official. Thus, he was not angered.

In fact, regarding the three disciples, the old deaf man would sooner or later need to discuss some clear matters with this young man, or else he wouldn’t feel at ease.

Chen Ping'an hesitated for a moment, then slammed his palm heavily on the ground, remaining motionless. No wonder this corpse, refined into a small world prison by the sword immortal, could trap those powerful demons.

Now, even the gods of the mountains and rivers in the Haoran realm are renowned for their indestructible golden bodies, but they cannot be said to possess any cultivation methods. Generally, they are nourished year after year by the incense of good men and women, like being coated in gold. The lifespan of mountain and river deities is indeed longer than that of cultivators. It is said that many earth immortals, unable to break through the bottleneck of the great way, would go to extreme lengths to forcefully extend their lives, even colluding with the government and local officials, helping to conceal Confucian academies, secretly building lewd shrines. If they had bad luck and could not withstand the trials of being worn down to bone and having their souls scattered, everything would naturally come to an end. But if they were lucky enough to pull through, their path of cultivation could transition from immortal to divine, allowing them to enjoy the incense of the world. 

Wei Ban should be the exception.

However, Chen Ping'an would never inquire about the many secrets of this former god of the Water Nation and the Mountain Sovereign. Zhu Lian and Zheng Dafeng were old hands in this regard, so the Cloudy Peak and the Fallen Mountain shared a tacit understanding.

Finally, the old deaf man spoke, "Nianxin is probably around seven to eight hundred years old now. She has stumbled her way to the upper fifth realm, and her talent is exceptional. However, consecutive breakthroughs have harmed her essence, so at this moment, she's in the Jade Purity realm and can only rely on unconventional methods, along with the haphazard accumulation of divine money and magical items, to maintain her current level. In her lifetime, unless something extraordinary happens, she will likely stop here. Nianxin has no clear lineage, and is mostly a wild cultivator who just happened to climb the mountain through unconventional means; otherwise, she wouldn’t have such a rough path."

"But she has no intention of reaching the peak. After avenging her great grievances in Golden Armor Continent, she thought she would die without regrets. Unexpectedly, she heard some dubious rumors that the city lord of White Emperor City has an interest in her. Not wanting to fall into a fate worse than death, she fled to the Upside-Down Mountain. Originally, she wanted to sneak over to the Wild World, where the situation is more chaotic, and her skills would find a place to shine. If she were to run into a dead end, who knows, she might even break through. Who would have thought she was intercepted by a sword immortal and thrown here?"

"While here, she hasn’t been idle. Many of the bodies of powerful demons were disassembled and sent to the alchemy workshop by her. Her techniques are exquisite and save the alchemists a lot of trouble."

Much of the inside scoop was heard by the old deaf man from that white-haired boy.

The old deaf man himself was never concerned with these convoluted stories of others; whether he knew or not wouldn’t reduce his weight, and knowing wouldn’t add an extra jar of wine.

Chen Ping'an withdrew his hand and rose, curious as he asked, “The city lord of White Emperor City would be interested in a seamstress?”

It was not that Chen Ping'an held any prejudice against Nianxin or seamstresses. There are many wild fox Zen teachings in the world, and there are distinctions in the cultivation methods. However, the majesty of that demonic giant towered above the clouds. As a recognized figure of the demonic path, he could still enjoy a reputation across the world. Chen Ping'an had some thoughts early on, including a firm desire to see the torrent of the Yellow River cave heavens and the banner of "First in the World" of White Emperor City during his travels in the Central Divine Continent.

Cui Zhan had once mentioned the colorful cloud spectrum beneath him, and even though Cui Dongshan often spoke of that city lord, it was hard for him to hide his admiration.

Mr. Qi had also traveled alongside the great river, where the city lord had famously left White Emperor City in the colorful clouds to personally invite him for a game of chess.

Such a perceptive giant of the demonic path would be sincerely addressed as Senior by Chen Ping'an, who naturally did not feel he had the qualifications to meet that city lord.

The old deaf man shook his head and explained, “Hidden Official, you truly underestimate Nianxin. She’s no ordinary seamstress. Early on, when she was merely in the Golden Core guest realm, she possessed the means of the Jade Purity realm. A few of her spells and divine abilities, once fully unleashed, could make even an enlightened Jade Purity realm practitioner find it hard to handle.”

Chen Ping'an couldn't help but recall the incident in the canyon of Beiju Luzhou, where the assassins from Ge Deer Mountain had ambushed him. The perilousness of that battle, in Chen Ping'an's heart, was not inferior at all to the encirclement of Li Zhenyu's group.

The old deaf man chuckled, “Otherwise, how could a mere Yuan Ying practitioner alone bring down a sect in Golden Armor Continent? If it were the Hidden Official, it wouldn’t be possible either, would it?”

Chen Ping'an was greatly surprised, unable to believe it as he asked, “A Yuan Ying practitioner could single-handedly destroy an entire sect?”

The old deaf man said lightly, “In less than half a year, all seven hundred of them, including the entire Ancestor Hall, were wiped out. A rather large sect, whose incense was entirely severed.”

Chen Ping'an squinted, “How did Nianxin escape such a calamity to reach the Upside-Down Mountain?”

The old deaf man shook his head, “Why should I care about that?”

Chen Ping'an laughed, “True, why should I care about that? But if I have the chance, I’d like to learn more from Senior Nianxin.”

The old deaf man became interested, “As a Confucian disciple, do you have personal grudges?”

Chen Ping'an said, “There are a few.”

The old deaf man chuckled, “I suppose they didn’t offer enough incense.”

Chen Ping'an was unwilling to delve into that, frowning as he asked, “What about the external heavenly demon?”

The old deaf man shook his head, “Can’t say. If it’s not a business matter, Hidden Official, please don’t make it hard for me.”

Chen Ping'an then asked, “Why does an external heavenly demon wear a green snake crown and a short sword?”

In Chen Ping'an's eyes, that white-haired boy seemed no different from a human, and the other party did not use any illusions.

The old deaf man’s expression was playful, “He likes to show off.”

Chen Ping'an shook his head, “Too reckless.”

The old deaf man chuckled.

In this prison, who was he being cautious for?

Chen Ping'an did not pursue the matter further and changed the subject, “Besides Nianxin and the external heavenly demon, does Senior have any other guests?”

The old deaf man nodded, “There’s also a sorrowful man who loves wine and gambling.”

Of course, he was also quite wealthy.

The old deaf man asked, “Young Hidden Official, are you asking for the cultivation methods of the demon race because there are demon creatures in your hometown worth cultivating?”

Chen Ping'an shook his head, “It’s not about cultivation; having more self-protection methods is always good.”

On the Fallen Mountain, the growth of plants was all natural.

The old deaf man waved his hand, and a large demon of the Jade Purity realm shifted its massive body closer to the sword-light barrier. The old deaf man reached out, tearing off a large chunk of bloody meat and slowly chewing on it. Since there was a young Hidden Official nearby, he covered his mouth with his hand as a gesture of hospitality.

Stepping out of the prison together, Chen Ping'an began to wander through the ancient battlefield littered with corpses, with the old deaf man as his host.

The old deaf man asked, “Hidden Official, with the war at Sword Qi Great Wall approaching, are we just going to wander around like this without thinking about returning to the Summer Resort Palace to handle affairs?”

Chen Ping'an lowered his gaze, “No rush.”

The young man slowly raised his eyes, “In fact, I don’t really want to go there.”

Every day spent there was not easy for any sword cultivator of the Hidden Official lineage, let alone Chen Ping'an.

The Big Sword Immortal had previously mentioned that in the coming battle, the Summer Resort Palace should not intervene too much.

They needed to give all the sword cultivators of Sword Qi Great Wall the opportunity to wield their swords freely.

He, Chen Qingdu, would not impose restrictions, and the Hidden Official lineage should also manage less.

Chen Ping'an had no objections.

He looked toward a colossal demon corpse ahead, its bones were too pale, lacking the “vitality” of the luminous white bones of Ghostly Valley. If it were moved to the desolate wilds of the Haoran realm, exposed to the wind and sun, it would likely weather away in just a few years. Simply put, these giant demon corpses were not worth much. On the other hand, those divine beings’ remaining golden bodies, while seemingly sturdy, still evoked a sense of indestructibility, shining golden, with only a few holes that were negligible compared to their massive forms. Unfortunately, it was just an illusion, and they still could not transform into the divine money of the Summer Resort Palace, not counting as part of the assets of Sword Qi Great Wall.

The old deaf man remarked on these ancient gods, though once respected and powerful, they were now pitiful creatures who had reached the end of the great way. Once the golden body showed signs of decay, even the slightest flaw would mean the divine being officially stepped into oblivion, with no hope of reversal.

Chen Ping'an uttered a word: merit.

The old deaf man nodded, “This is the remedy of the three teachings’ sages for future deities and the key to stabilizing several realms.”

Deities of mountains and rivers, conferred by the court and recognized by Confucian academies, had always been crucial bridges connecting the ordinary scholars with cultivators, preventing constant direct conflicts. The numerous local lewd shrines, regardless of the reasons behind the court’s neglect or the Confucian academies' lack of inquiry, were naturally valued for their role in mending local customs and promoting goodness.

As they walked to a place where a deity was extraordinarily tall, half of its body submerged in the sea of clouds, its entirety was unseen.

Chen Ping'an slightly bent his knees, suddenly exerted force, and leapt into the sea of clouds.

With his hands tucked into his sleeves and his feet floating, he leapt out of the sea of clouds, finally seeing the solemn face of the deity. Chen Ping'an stood upon the Pine Needle and Thunder Sword, hanging over the sea of clouds.

His heart grew heavy, “That sword cultivator, Yu Si?”

Surrounding the deity, numerous green water droplets, naturally formed, floated in the sea of clouds, accumulating to over a hundred. The richness of the water was incredible, clearly unrefined, and its quality approached that of water elixirs produced in ordinary water temples, though it could not be compared to the dragon water elixir gifted by Real Person Fire Dragon. Nevertheless, for any water deities, river goddesses, and Qi practitioners, these water droplets were considered treasures, especially since they were easy to obtain and abundant. Any sect would covet them.

It was said that if the Rain Dragon Sect, located next to Jiao Long Gully, could move this god statue and make it the core of their mountain and water great formation, their sect’s power could directly rise a whole level.

Chen Ping'an felt a sense of resonance with this deity, as its aura reminded him of the young sword cultivator, Yu Si.

The old deaf man stood by, nodding as he said, “Quite a background. The Hidden Official is indeed the Hidden Official, never striking down nameless enemies.”

Chen Ping'an helplessly said, “A small Jia Shen tent, hidden dragons and crouching tigers.”

The old deaf man gleefully remarked, “With the Hidden Official winning three consecutive battles, I suppose the world back home wouldn’t dare believe it.”

Chen Ping'an asked, “So that boy in the water prison is made up of these water droplets?”

The old deaf man casually admitted, “That’s right.”

Raising dragons is a high threshold; one must first find suitable dragon-like creatures to cultivate, then have a method to raise them, and finally, know how to create dragon ponds.

Coincidentally, the old deaf man lacked none of these.

Every ascended great cultivator’s path could indeed make for an extremely exciting strange tale.

Chen Ping'an turned to ask, “If it were you taking action, how did those demon race practitioners die?”

The old deaf man casually replied, “With a flick of my finger.”

With the complete cultivation of a transcendent realm, dealing with prisoners who were at most in the immortal realm, the old deaf man held the advantage of time, place, and people in his little world. It was indeed a matter of just a finger flick.

Then the old man added, “If there was any noise, any curses or pleas for mercy, they would probably die a slower death. I had a little free time and learned some skin-pulling techniques from that young girl.”

Chen Ping'an mused, “Having stayed too long in Sword Qi Great Wall, I almost forgot that sword immortals are sword immortals, and great demons are great demons.”

He still vividly remembered the first time he met the Sword Immortal Ji Yue in Yuanting Mountain, feeling apprehensive and walking on thin ice. One misstep could lead to doom.

Even earlier, on that ferry from Jiao Mountain, he had witnessed the three sword challenges between Fenglei Yard and Zhengyang Mountain, where Yuan Ying Li Tuanjing’s closing sword was simply magnificent.

Even further back, on a night of heavy rain, he had taken shelter in an ancient residence and encountered a powerful demon of the middle fifth realm from the Ancient Elm Kingdom.

What a fleeting moment this was.

Chen Ping'an said, “Senior, you can just collect this water fortune, and I can turn a blind eye.”

Before Chen Ping'an’s eyes, the old deaf man extracted dozens of pale green water droplets, using the method of space within his sleeve to collect them. They should all have been the most abundant in water fortune.

Then Chen Ping'an opened his mouth to ask for half of the water droplets, most of which he stored in his Sword Cultivation Gourd, leaving only three droplets. He sat cross-legged and began to refine them openly, following the incantation inscribed on the rain prayer stele outside the Water God Shrine.

This was a fair division of the natural fortune. 

The old deaf man accepted this without hesitation.

The old deaf man glanced at the basic workings of Chen Ping'an’s water refining technique and praised, “With this method alone, if you are ever driven to a corner, you can discard your physical form and choose a river near a great lake to become a river god.”

Chen Ping'an remained focused, refining those three droplets that equated to ordinary water elixirs at an extremely fast pace. Over at the Water God side, it was like a long-awaited rain, as the green-clad boys became busy repairing the flaws in their water character talismans, restoring the nearly faded murals in the Water God Shrine to color, and the dried-up small pond began to flow with fresh water again.

As Chen Ping'an slightly diverted his attention to speak, he cautioned, “I advise Senior not to go to the Haoran realm.”

The old deaf man asked, “Why?”

Chen Ping'an fell silent.

The white-haired boy appeared on the deity’s shoulder and sneered, “Old deaf man, you’re too good at flattery; you’ll probably get torn apart and minced into meat paste.”

Then the white-haired boy mocked, “You young man, your mind isn’t sharp enough. That old deaf man deliberately picked some water droplets with thin spiritual energy, knowing you would ask for them. On the sea of clouds, the water droplets keep appearing; he would definitely have deliberately missed the ones with the most abundant water fortune every time. What a little fool you are, how can you be a Hidden Official? You’re leagues behind Xiao Xian, no wonder the Sword Qi Great Wall can’t hold up.”

Chen Ping'an ignored him.

The old deaf man remained indifferent, offering no explanations.

In any case, if that external heavenly demon ever found an opening to disturb the young Hidden Official's spirit, the old deaf man wouldn’t stand idly by.

That mysterious external heavenly demon was capricious, suddenly enraged, and indignantly said, “Even the Confucian disciples of Haoran realm are so treacherous, they deserve to be pillaged by the demon race of the Wild World. It’s time to change the customs!”

Chen Ping'an took out more water droplets from his Sword Cultivation Gourd, each one refined into his own water fortune.

A proper fifth realm Qi practitioner, just one step away from the middle fifth realm immortal, would indeed possess greater skill than a third realm practitioner.

The white-haired boy seemed to sense the young Hidden Official's state of mind and began cursing loudly, “You shameless thing, a mere fifth realm practitioner, how dare you feel satisfied?!”

In the next moment, the boy suddenly fell silent, sitting cross-legged again and slowly said, “That Chen fellow, with a full heart, is a good candidate for cultivation. I have five superior techniques that directly lead to the upper fifth realm, the most profound ones. If you have those five elemental life objects as a foundation, it would be twice the result with half the effort. Do you want to learn? I can swear, as long as you nod in agreement, there will be absolutely no hidden dangers. If you don’t believe me, you can ask the old deaf man; I assure you can quickly reach the Jade Purity realm. This is a no-risk deal; do you want to do it?!”

Chen Ping'an opened his eyes and asked with a smile, “Do you think your methods are superior to Lu Chen’s?”

The white-haired boy burst into laughter, and in an instant, a young Daoist wearing a lotus crown appeared on the deity’s shoulder, smiling without speaking.

Chen Ping'an and the old deaf man asked, “With all this uproar, is there no one to restrain you?”

The old deaf man nodded, “There is.”

A sharp sword light suddenly arrived, shattering the figure of “Lu Chen” like ice being smashed by a hammer.

The white-haired boy gathered his form far away, unscathed, but his robe was in tatters. He no longer spoke, as if he had made an agreement with the master of the sword light.

He glared in the direction of a certain place and then transformed into a rainbow light, heading towards a nearby deity's corpse, drawing his sword from its sheath, and began "digging," using the short sword like a chisel and his palm as a hammer. It made a ringing sound as countless fragments flew, dust swirling, until he finally dug out a piece the size of a chestnut of the golden body fragment, crushing it in his palm, and casually applying it to his robe, the golden light flowing like water, as if alive, self-repairing the robe.

Chen Ping'an whispered, “The forging material for the military armor must be fragments of divine bodies, right?”

The three types of military armors, including the Shenren Chengluo armor, had no written records in the various books of the Haoran realm about what heavenly materials they were forged from. Chen Ping'an had never asked Cui Dongshan or Wei Ban about it before. As for the origin of the gold essence copper coins, that was already confirmed. Once the Lotus Root Blessed Land reached the middle blessed land, in addition to divine money, it also required a large amount of gold essence copper coins.

The old deaf man nodded, “The forging process of military armors is complex; the fundamental material is indeed fragments of golden bodies.”

The Big Sword Immortal suddenly appeared beside Chen Ping'an.

But the next moment, he was shattered by sword light again.

Then that white-haired boy, who had just excavated the second piece of golden body fragment, darted towards the prison entrance, but halfway there, he was again slashed to pieces by sword light.

At the prison side, peering in, sword light struck again, forcing the white-haired boy to sit on the steps, continuing to patch his robe with that palm-sized fragment of golden body.

The old deaf man chuckled, “After breaking the contract, he can only stay in the prison for a decade.”

Chen Ping'an helplessly said, “Isn’t this more troublesome for me? Could I trouble that sword immortal senior to change his punishment?”

The old deaf man replied, “As long as there’s wine, it’s fine.”

Chen Ping'an felt a bit regretful.

He had come in a hurry, and there were only two jars of wine left.

He was reluctant to part with them.

Especially after seeing Nianxin, these two jars of wine could not be given away.

With the entanglement of that external heavenly demon, it was just as well to sharpen his Dao heart.

Unexpectedly, an omen appeared as the Big Sword Immortal slowly walked out of the prison, holding the neck of that external heavenly demon like a chick.

This time, he seemed far less indifferent than when facing the sword light, with the white-haired boy trembling in the Big Sword Immortal’s grip, filled with fear.

Yet Chen Ping'an suspected whether this scene was an illusion created by that external heavenly demon on purpose.

But he quickly confirmed that the Big Sword Immortal was not some illusion.

For on the surface of Chen Ping'an's heart lake, there was a piece of paper manifested by the Big Sword Immortal, documenting many of the sword immortal's arrangements.

As soon as Chen Ping'an finished reading, that paper dissolved into nothingness.

Regarding the future paths of the young talented sword cultivators outside of the Sword Immortal of the Sword Qi Great Wall, the Big Sword Immortal had already made a decision, clearly stating it to Chen Ping'an. Chen Ping'an made some slight modifications, and the Big Sword Immortal agreed to some, while rejecting others.

After Chen Ping'an saw this piece of paper, he became increasingly clear about the Big Sword Immortal's intentions.

It was almost in line with his own speculations.

The three old sword immortals carving characters on the city wall—Qi Tingji, after the great battle, left alone for Fuyiao Continent with no one from the Qi Clan’s lineage to accompany him. 

Qi Tingji would need to guard that mountain and water cave for a hundred years, after which he would be free. If the demon race took Fuyiao Continent, Qi Tingji wouldn’t be able to seek refuge in the Wild World either, digging a hole to hide.

Chen Xi would engage in a fierce battle, reincarnating through the method of military dissolution, with his soul gathered in a lamp of his life, taken by other sword cultivators to the Fifth World. Although he could be born with knowledge, he still needed a guardian.

As for Dong Sangeng, he wouldn’t leave. Life and death were in his hometown.

Nalan Shaowei would also die by military dissolution, with his life lamp taken by a guardian to the Qingming realm. Although the path of cultivation after military dissolution would be greatly obstructed, achieving the great way would be incredibly difficult, it was still better than dying and disappearing.

The old deaf man had chosen to rely on the old blind man rather than follow the demon army to the Haoran realm, working hard in the Ten Thousand Mountains.

The reasoning was simple; he was afraid of death.

Many ascended great cultivators were so reluctant to part with their lives that it reached an astonishing degree. Du Mao from the Tongye Sect was the best example; he could go to any lengths, with no means spared.

Sects, offspring, disciples, reputation—everything could be sacrificed.

As for Lu Zhi, the path was paved by Chen Ping'an, and in addition to Lu Zhi, Madam Chuan Yan and Shao Yunyan from Chuan Fan Studio would accompany Lu Zhi.

Connecting to the earlier arrangements made by the Big Sword Immortal for the young sword cultivators, Chen Ping'an finally confirmed a principle.

Almost everyone was destined to part ways.

From now on, it would be a true separation, and in this sense, their cultivation levels would represent a kind of reunion.

For example, Qi Tingji would go to Fuyiao Continent, while Qi Shou would remain at Upside-Down Mountain.

Chen Xi would go to the Fifth World, but Chen Sanqiu would travel through the Haoran realm.

Meanwhile, the high-ranking Marquis Gao Ye, accompanying Chen Xi, would have his sister Gao Youqing become the direct disciple of Floating Sword Lake’s Li Cai, heading to Beiju Luzhou.

The next great battle would also be the last battle for Sword Qi Great Wall in ten thousand years.

For those who were not sword cultivators, it didn’t matter; they could just avoid it. However, in the future, as the battle approached its climax, there would inevitably be demon race survivors slipping through to the north of the city wall, and not everyone would survive.

Lower fifth realm sword cultivators. Those who are willing to die will die, engaging in battle on the city wall; those lacking the ability will still die. But as long as they can hold on until the end, they can preserve their lives and future paths.

Middle fifth realm sword cultivators. Those who wish to live will live. Those who cannot die will find it impossible even if they want to.

Only the upper fifth realm sword immortals. Life and death are not under their control, and the Big Sword Immortal has long since made arrangements.

The Big Sword Immortal stepped out from the top of the prison steps, throwing down the white-haired boy he was holding, and asked, “Tired of living?”

The external heavenly demon lay prostrate on the ground, facing the old deaf man and the young Hidden Official with a sense of freedom, yet at this moment, it could only shake its head, not daring to speak.

A figure shrouded in mist appeared next to Chen Qingdu, with only a long sword clearly visible.

Chen Qingdu said, “If you don’t drink, you won’t have the energy; swinging your sword will be like sewing flowers?”

The reprimanded peculiar sword immortal remained silent.

Chen Ping'an and the old deaf man approached the Big Sword Immortal.

Chen Qingdu brought the two young men into this realm, causing them to fall to the ground, vomiting.

Chen Ping'an only recognized one of them, an inconspicuous third realm sword cultivator from Sword Qi Great Wall, with an ordinary background and talent. The boy was responsible for distributing the workshop robes and long swords on the city wall and often carried injured sword cultivators away.

As for the other boy, Chen Ping'an had no impression of him at all.

Chen Qingdu spoke to the old deaf man and the sword immortal, “You keep them by your side for a hundred years, serving as your masters, and thereafter, do as you wish.”

The old deaf man did not dare to refuse.

The unseen sword immortal also remained silent.

For the two boys, it was a tremendous opportunity.

Chen Qingdu looked at the external heavenly demon lying on the ground, “Shouldn’t you speak when it’s time to?”

The white-haired boy quickly sat up and said with righteous indignation, “Hidden Official should feel resentful; working hard for who? Aren’t I making clothes for others more than that seamstress? Such great fortune, why does it fall on two little brats inferior to pigs and dogs? Chen Qingdu, you’re being unjust; why not simply revolt against Sword Qi Great Wall and scheme for a position that’s not inferior to that of a Hidden Official? That would be a real man’s behavior…”

Chen Ping'an raised his hand to his forehead.

One boy, who would become an attendant of a sword immortal inexplicably, looked extremely anxious, while the other, destined to be the master of the old deaf man, remained calm.

The sword immortal removed his sword and gifted it to the boy.

The old deaf man smiled at the nominal master.

Chen Qingdu led Chen Ping'an back toward the prison.

Chen Qingdu slowly said, “If it weren’t for being here, the one speaking with you now would be that external heavenly demon. Life is a dream within a dream. From the moment you began to gather your mind to refine the water droplets, you would have been taken advantage of. Don’t believe it? You think you’re sufficiently vigilant against that external heavenly demon? Then try it.”

Chen Ping'an suddenly halted, summoning his life sword, the Caged Sparrow.

Then it was as if he abruptly awoke from a dream.

Chen Ping'an looked around, realizing he was still sitting cross-legged, refining water droplets. 

The old deaf man was still smiling beside him.

The white-haired boy, wearing a green snake crown and holding a short sword, was still sitting cross-legged on the deity’s shoulder.

Yet, the Caged Sparrow’s small world did not exist.

It was an illusory scene.

Chen Ping'an felt as if he had fallen into an ice cave.

The world changed again.

He stood beneath the prison, where he first saw the seamstress, Nianxin. She still gracefully performed a deep bow, but when she raised her head, her eyes were filled with mischief. “Am I the fake? Is she definitely the real one?”

In the next moment, Chen Ping'an found himself locking eyes with that boy in the water prison. The boy stood up and smiled slightly, “Are you sure that killing me will spare the Haoran realm from a disaster?”

In another instant, he returned to the sea of clouds, where the “young Daoist Lu Chen” stood on the deity's shoulder, smiling, “Is my Dao method high?”

Before Chen Ping'an could even think, he found himself at the entrance of the prison, where the sword immortal shrouded in mist slowly revealed half his face, saying, “Aren’t you curious why my blurry image appears? Is it because the face of the sword immortal in your heart is manifesting?”

Scenes continuously appeared around Chen Ping'an, though they were accompanied by additional words.

The old deaf man stood beneath the stone tablet of the Zhaotian Temple and slowly spoke, “Hidden Official, as a direct disciple of the Sage of Literature, your knowledge seems insufficient.”

At the entrance of the prison, the Big Sword Immortal held the white-haired boy by the neck, slowly walking to the top of the steps, suddenly laughing, “Did you really think Chen Qingdu had such divine powers? Who would have thought the Hidden Official held such deep admiration for the Big Sword Immortal, only he seems to have a bad temper?”

The two boys were captured from Sword Qi Great Wall into this small world by the Big Sword Immortal. Among them, the more timid boy suddenly smiled, “So the young master in Hidden Official's heart should be so earnest in doing good.”

The other boy shook his head, “That’s not right, not right at all. Even if he is young, he should be as steady as I am; otherwise, he won’t live long.”

Even secretly condensing his heart into a mustard seed and heading to the Water God, those green-clad boys gathered outside the Water God’s gate, all bearing the visage of the external heavenly demon.

Chen Ping'an’s head began to throb unbearably.

Teetering, he returned to the steps, sitting down, and summoned his life sword, the Caged Sparrow, but to his astonishment, hadn’t he already summoned it earlier?

Looking up, the figure of Chen Qingdu at the bottom of the steps turned around and asked, “How is it?”

Chen Ping'an was at a loss for words.

“Chen Qingdu” smiled, “You think you’ve seen through me as an illusion, and you’ve won? Have you really stepped out of the prison? Are you certain you’ve truly been to Sword Qi Great Wall? How do you know that everything today is merely a yellowing dream gifted to you by Lu Chen? Could you still be in your hometown, in the Mud Bottle Alley? How can you be certain it isn’t a fish from the bank observing people? Could you be someone’s dream-walking perspective?”

Chen Ping'an closed his eyes, took a deep breath, and punched himself hard to knock himself out.

On the steps, the white-haired boy crouched nearby, muttering, “Taking shortcuts is not honorable; I’d better not delay his serious matters.”

Chen Qingdu frowned.

The young man, having knocked himself out, was not a big deal; it was the right choice.

However, if he were awakened by an outsider’s punch, it might lead to significant risks.

The white-haired boy angrily said, “It really has nothing to do with me.”

In the end, the young man fell into a sweet dream, sleeping soundly, his breathing incredibly steady, as if dreaming of a wonderful dream he did not want to wake from.

Chen Qingdu grabbed the white-haired boy by the head and lifted him up, saying in a deep voice, “You go take a look, what exactly is happening.”

The external heavenly demon muttered, then Chen Qingdu tightened his grip, and it suddenly howled in pain, having to flash away into the young man’s dream.

Moments later, it exited the dream, helplessly saying, “How strange, there’s nothing unusual; just a little kid bouncing around in a small alley, full of smiles, then it transformed into a snowy little courtyard. The child hasn’t grown much but appears quite happy, and these two scenes keep cycling, unchanging, just these two scrolls.”

The old deaf man tentatively asked, “In the scroll, is there anyone else? Can you manifest someone to break the dream with words?”

The white-haired boy shook his head, “Difficult. The scroll is too hazy; this is a small world, separated from the Haoran realm by a large world. This kid’s hometown seems to be another small world, and I’m not familiar with this child’s life. How could I manage that? If I were to act, it could easily cause him to sink deeper into it, and then it would be beyond even the divine’s rescue.”

In an instant, Chen Ping'an opened his eyes, suddenly sitting up, drenched in sweat.

Chen Qingdu breathed a sigh of relief, asking, “How did you exit the dream?”

Chen Ping'an remained silent.

Chen Qingdu shook his head, sighing, “You should now have an idea of how difficult it will be to reach the upper fifth realm.”

Chen Ping'an nodded, wiping the sweat from his forehead.

Chen Qingdu glanced at the external heavenly demon, who immediately assured, “This kid will be my grandpa from now on; I promise not to mess around.”

Chen Qingdu left with the old deaf man and Nianxin, while the white-haired boy did not dare stay longer, fearing that Chen Qingdu might take out his frustrations on him, leaving only Chen Ping'an behind.

After they left, Chen Ping'an began to smile.

He had a wonderful dream, and in the end, he dreamt of someone bowing and someone returning the gesture, so the former was unaware.

It was his younger self, then still carrying a big basket.

Mr. Qi bowed and returned the greeting, smiling and speaking to his disciples as they bid farewell.

Chen Ping'an could not remember such a thing, only knowing that he had indeed thanked Mr. Qi in a bow back then.

What else could it be but a good dream?

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 789: Needlework

Chen Ping'an sat on the steps, rolled up his trousers, and took off his boots, placing them among the white jade artifacts. 

The other two artifacts he possessed—one borrowed from Yan Ming—had already been sent to the alchemy workshop for repairs by a master craftsman. The remaining Daoist talisman artifact was obtained through a trade with Sun Qing, the lord of the Colorful Sparrow House, and he had additionally made a profit of thirty Grain Rain Coins. If all merchants in the world were as straightforward as those from the Colorful Sparrow House, Chen Ping'an wouldn't mind carrying a whole building on his back, let alone a piece of the Zaojing (a type of Daoist artifact). Of course, if that building could be refined into a bonsai like Chunfan Studio or the Plum Blossom Garden, that would be even better.

The artifact related to the Daoist Sun from the Qingming Realm had already been entrusted to A Liang for delivery to a Daoist sage.

At this moment, Chen Ping'an's current artifact had passed through the Sword-Cultivating Pavilion, where he collected all the sword immortals' portraits. Afterward, it was claimed by the senior sword immortal, and when it was returned, it had already been set with a secret restriction that even Chen Ping'an, as its owner, couldn't unlock. He was unsure what the senior sword immortal was up to.

Walking along this so-called "Divine Path," he made his way to the bottom of the prison, gently rolling up his sleeves.

A human body is a small universe; the universe is a large human body.

This saying cannot simply be generalized in Daoist terms.

This nameless prison, along with six powerful demons of the Upper Five Realms, held a total of seventy demon cultivators. Leaving aside the three of the Lower Five Realms, the majority were Earth Immortals, all fierce individuals who would likely stand out as heroes in the Barbaric or the Hao Ran realms. Without exception, they had all fought against sword cultivators on the battlefield, many having destroyed more than one of their life swords.

As Chen Ping'an continued on his way, it seemed that without the old deaf man around, several previously silent Upper Five Realm demons emerged from the misty barriers of their cages, approaching the sword light barrier. Whether in true form or human guise, they scrutinized the young man in a green robe, barefoot, with rolled sleeves, who could still speak the refined language of the Barbaric Realm.

One of the demons, transformed into a middle-aged man, stood close to the prison bars. He used an illusion technique, donning a long green robe that gave him a scholarly appearance. With a bamboo flute at his waist, his demeanor was as graceful as moonlight lingering through the ages. He lightly tapped a streak of sword light with his finger, and where it met, flesh and blood melded together, producing a strange, fragrant aroma that was completely devoid of any meaty scent. He asked with a smile, "Young man, is the Sword Qi Great Wall about to fall?"

Chen Ping'an halted, meeting the gaze of the demon through the sword light barrier, and nodded, "For us, that's not good news."

According to the records of the Summer Palace, this demon had taken the name Yunqing, and his true form was a colorful phoenix. His feathers were exceptional materials for refining Daoist feather garments. Hence, when this demon reached the Upper Five Realms, he naturally possessed a robe equivalent to a half-immortal weapon. However, Yunqing's feathers took a long time to nurture; after seven hundred years of imprisonment, only seven had been collected, which had gradually been sold to three Daoist sects.

Yunqing smiled and asked, "Is Yueqing dead? Has Shouchen ascended to the Upper Five Realms?"

Chen Ping'an truthfully replied, "Yueqing is not dead. Shouchen is now the youngest sword immortal in your Barbaric Realm."

Yunqing nodded and thanked him, then his form melted back into the dense mist, seemingly sighing.

As he passed the next cage, a demon revealed its true form, furiously slamming against the sword light barrier. The barrier was unbreakable; within, the mist churned, and the demon's futile efforts only stirred a blood-soaked wind.

Big catfish in the mud feed on dragon-like creatures, seeking to transform into dragons.

Chen Ping'an asked, "Is there a shortcut for your water clan to transform into dragons? Like the celestial fox proving a path, only requiring the Heavenly Master’s seal on a fox skin to escape heavenly tribulations?"

Many ghosts and spirits cross rivers and climb mountains, needing to travel with those under the protection of virtuous merit to have a chance of evading the divine retribution of local gods. Countless spirits have found their paths blocked by mountains and waters. Moreover, it is said that many dragon-like creatures, when failing their journeys, would resort to various means to seek refuge—whether by seals, jade tokens, or even hiding within the lines of a sage's text. However, some matters Chen Ping'an had witnessed firsthand, while many others felt more like strange tales without the opportunity to verify.

Suddenly, the demon quieted down, slowly transforming back into human form, appearing as a gaunt old man. "Kid, trade me a pound of fresh blood!"

Chen Ping'an responded, "Half a pound."

The demon initially thought this was just a bit of fun, but to his surprise, the young man was serious in haggling?

The old man grasped the sword light bars tightly, his eyes sparkling with excitement as he laughed loudly, "Look at you, young lad, not too old yet but with quite the impressive vitality; your heart's essence blood is worth three coins. Blood from the organs connected to the soul is worth eight coins. Ordinary blood? At least a pound! If you give it willingly, I’ll teach you a priceless immortal technique. Not just the descendants of dragons, but any water clan spirit can transform into a dragon without issue."

Chen Ping'an remained silent, standing still. After a moment, he waited for the demon to show a hint of surprise before saying, “Is the opening technique from the Yeluo River really this trivial? I've seen your master’s methods; they’re not limited to just this.”

The demon before him had quietly unleashed a supernatural ability, a superior water ghost dragging technique. Spirits and demons would analyze one's heart through sight, and at the slightest stir of emotion, the organs would shake, and the soul would be captured, becoming a puppet. The Yeluo River was undoubtedly a vast water domain in the Barbaric Realm, where water clan spirits held great power.

Some water ghosts and water immortals in the great rivers favored using vile "replacement life techniques," dragging people underwater, flipping the yin and yang, often using this method to deceive the hearts of others. Hence, many who approached the water, once their yang energy was insufficient, ancestral blessings weak, and fortune lacking, would inexplicably find themselves entering the water.

The old man withdrew his injured hands, which healed rapidly, with the blood mist burned by the sword light not leaking outside the cage. He sneered, "If it weren't for the restrictions, just from smelling a hint of blood, you'd be lying on the ground right now, yearning for the immortal realm."

Chen Ping'an replied, "If I weren't a sword immortal, I would have already enjoyed a pot of catfish stew with tofu. Water ginseng is quite nourishing, and it can even sober one up."

The old man’s expression darkened.

This demon, known as Qingqiu in the Barbaric Realm, had a name that played on the word for "green catfish," which was a pity for such a good name.

Chen Ping'an asked, "Are we going to trade or not?"

The old man transformed again, the stench within the cage swirling as he revealed his true form, his eyes as large as lanterns, his massive head pressing against the sword light barrier, glaring at the young man without restraint.

Chen Ping'an turned to leave.

The demon said, "We are trading! I'm thirsty, so give me half a pound of fresh blood to quench my thirst! If it tastes good, I’ll take the other half pound from you and then tell you the shortcut for transforming into a dragon to escape disasters."

Seeing the young man nod, he continued on his way.

The demon slammed his head against the barrier, roaring, "How dare you mock your ancestor!"

Chen Ping'an turned back and said, "I’ll let the old deaf man come collect your three coins of heart essence blood. You better prepare a good excuse and don’t deceive me. You previously said half a pound of ordinary blood, and you didn't agree, so I don't understand—do you really conduct business like this?"

After Chen Ping'an left, the old deaf man stood outside the cage of the demon Qingqiu, laughing heartily, accompanied by a nearly oblivious youth named Youyu, whose name was strange, said to have been taken at random when he saw inscriptions in an alley. The other youth was named Du Shanyin. These two boys, who did not know each other, had entirely different attitudes toward the young Hidden Official; the former regarded him with awe, while the latter aspired to be like the Hidden Official, dreaming of it.

The demon Qingqiu, dealing with the barefooted young man, was quite "easygoing." Upon seeing the old deaf man, he immediately retreated into the misty barriers.

The old deaf man glanced at the mist within the cage and nodded, "So this catfish has the notion of water ginseng that can sober one up. I’ve learned something new."

Youyu whispered, "Hidden Official, your knowledge is vast."

The old deaf man laughed, "And he bears a grudge. Don't provoke scholars like this in the future."

The great demon Wangzu, the former master of the Yeluo River, had once slaughtered a South Traveling sword immortal surnamed Yue on the battlefield, leaving the Hidden Official in a precarious position at the Sword Qi Great Wall.

Thus, the young Hidden Official had been very polite to the demon Yunqing earlier, but upon encountering the mudfish, one of the four great horrors of the Yeluo River, he began to settle accounts, collecting a bit of interest—anything he could earn was worth it.

Youyu, feeling anxious, said, "Old deaf man, when I saw the Hidden Official, I didn't even dare to speak! How could I provoke someone who seems like a celestial being, I wouldn't dare! Moreover, the Hidden Official has exhausted himself for the Sword Qi Great Wall; I respect that. Now I regret being too timid and not speaking a word to him."

The Sword Qi Great Wall, when it comes to the youngest generation, each person might see the young Hidden Official differently.

For instance, Jiang Yun and Yuan Zao, the martial artists training in the streets, listened to the stories of mountains and waters from the second shopkeeper around the corner, while Sun Zao, who had never seen the young Hidden Official but had heard stories about him, along with Youyu and Du Shanyin, who were still young but could already slay demons atop the city wall.

The old deaf man said, "Fortune and misfortune come in waves; there's nothing to be afraid of."

Youyu nodded vigorously, "I'll remember that."

The old deaf man chuckled, "I wonder what the senior sword immortal thinks; you should trade with that ambitious Du Shanyin. You should get along well with that drunkard; perhaps your fortunes will grow in the future."

The youth's expression dimmed; he felt that his roots and disposition were too lacking, and he must have disappointed the old deaf man.

Chen Ping'an continued to walk at a leisurely pace, as if enjoying a mountain stroll.

A seven-tailed fox demon displayed all its tricks; as the young Hidden Official passed by, it shifted into several different forms in a short span, using its original appearance combined with illusion techniques. It transformed into a voluptuous woman with springtime beauty, a young maiden with light blush, a charming little nun, and even a cold-faced female Daoist. In the end, it even blurred its gender and turned into a graceful young man, kneeling and sitting by the sword light barrier, sobbing to seek favor.

Chen Ping'an ignored it, his heart like still water, observing like a dried-up bone.

Yet the fox demon remained undeterred; when the iron-hearted young man turned slightly away from the cage, it lunged forward, hands pressing against the ground, its voice soft and pleading, like weeping. Its back arched like rolling mountains.

Chen Ping'an walked straight past.

Upon reaching the fourth-to-last prison, he encountered a practitioner of the Dragon Gate Realm. Skilled at concealing his aura, his trump card was two artifacts capable of binding life swords, a ruthless individual who relished in slaughtering sword cultivators on the battlefield.

Regarding such actions, Chen Ping'an had no strong feelings. On the Sword Qi Great Wall, several sword immortals, including Nalan Caihuan and Qi Shou, were renowned for their brutal methods. However, according to the records of the Hidden Official lineage, this practitioner from the major sect of the Barbaric Realm was infamous among the demons for his cruelty, especially fond of purchasing bamboo coffins, considered "mongrels" in the Barbaric Realm, and had even purchased several female sword cultivator captives from the mountain where the great demon Chongguang resided. One could imagine their fate.

Chen Ping'an softly said, "Senior Lianxin, help me open the door."

He knew the prison’s restrictions and the secret arts to open them but could not do so.

The seamstress's figure appeared, and the sword light barrier vanished in an instant.

As Chen Ping'an stepped forward, he noticed she had no intention of leaving. Standing at the doorway with his back to the pitiful woman, he was about to speak.

Lianxin remarked, "Is the Hidden Official overestimating himself? Or is it that out of face, he doesn’t wish for others to see the cruel methods of a Confucian disciple? There’s no need."

Chen Ping'an nodded, rolling up another layer of his sleeves.

About a stick of incense later.

Lianxin glanced at the figure squatting on the ground.

The Dragon Gate Realm demon was left with only its head intact; everything below the neck was a messy pile of flesh, yet it was not dead. The flesh, bones, and soul were layered, and the methods were gentle.

It seemed the young Hidden Official had faced considerable hardship in his martial path, truly embodying the saying "a long illness makes one a skilled doctor."

Even the demon of the Dragon Gate Realm, with a resilient body and spirit, was pleading, "Kill me, kill me."

Chen Ping'an merely gouged out one of the demon's eyes, gently crushed it, and rubbed his fingers over its forehead, asking, "Is this demon's human form each quite different?"

Lianxin nodded, "Not only do demons differ in their transformations, but we, too, studying the laws of the world, share the same origin yet diverge into countless branches. Those methods that can be deemed 'authentic and transcendent' are those that can minimize the influence of detours. The righteous path is paramount, while the secondary paths are lesser, and the evil paths are even less so; they can still ascend the mountain, but the difficulty varies. The more authentic one is, the more accurately they can grasp the intricacies of the human body as a hidden paradise, minimizing detours. The simpler the reasoning, the wider the road, and the more spiritual energy flows, like a grand army, with great momentum. If it’s a narrow and rugged path, the flow of spiritual energy will inevitably be limited. However, nothing is absolute; extraordinary talents are not bound by this principle, and even narrow paths can lead to the peak."

Chen Ping'an extended a finger to the demon's forehead and gently traced downwards, as if slicing with a knife, then carefully peeled back its skin.

Lianxin observed his movements, slow yet steady, and most importantly, his heart was undisturbed, without resentment or joy, making him a natural fit as both a seamstress and executioner.

Among the ten types of cultivators listed in the Hao Ran realm, the executioners and seamstresses shared many similarities.

Lianxin advised, "Killing such a frail Dragon Gate demon isn't worthy of me getting involved in sewing."

Chen Ping'an nodded, "Understood. I just want to warm up, as I plan to learn sewing skills from Senior Lianxin."

Lianxin shook her head, "I advise the Hidden Official not to delve into this too easily; it will only earn the hatred of heaven and earth, obstructing the Dao. A martial artist becoming a deity, a sword cultivator ascending to the heavens, is the true path the Hidden Official should take."

Chen Ping'an pointed at the demon cultivator's forehead, rising slowly, "There are no taboos in techniques; as long as one's heart is settled, evil people will have their own way of dealing with evil people. There's a subtle difference in wording between the two statements; the former is too helpless, while the latter is too absolute, and I feel both are incorrect."

Lianxin remained silent.

Chen Ping'an exited the prison, heading to the next cage.

According to the records of the Summer Palace, he simply threw punches at will.

Different techniques shared one similarity: one would always introduce themselves first.

In the Hao Ran realm, Chen Ping'an.

Lianxin followed closely behind the young man, observing the entire process from beginning to end.

When slaying the Earth Immortal demon, Lianxin would open her embroidered pouch, taking out various fine needles and short blades to handle the corpse, while the young Hidden Official stood by, watching.

Lianxin's yin spirit emerged, a peculiar sight, as tiny as a mustard seed, almost invisible, holding an even smaller artifact, a "sewing needle."

When facing a demon of the Golden Core Realm, Chen Ping'an allowed the opponent to unleash their full power without retaliating.

When confronting a sword cultivator of the Golden Core Realm, Lianxin was astonished to see the young Hidden Official vanish into thin air, seemingly creating a small universe.

After removing the life sword's innate abilities, Chen Ping'an observed Lianxin processing the corpse, asking, "Senior Lianxin, among the ten types of Qi cultivators, how many have you personally witnessed, including seamstresses?"

Lianxin continued her motions, skillfully selecting tendons and bones, extracting them with fluidity, though it had little to do with aesthetic pleasure.

Lianxin shared some secrets not recorded in the Summer Palace's texts. Those who refined ancient tombs and graves, invoking the passage of “transients,” when high-level, could tear apart their life flags, risking everything to alter the heavens, turning vast areas into realms of darkness.

Additionally, there were the seductive corpses, whose charm surpassed that of fox demons, half-human, half-ghost, undetectable by immortals, who most enjoyed indulging in palace debauchery. However, seductive corpses rarely appeared, but each time they did, they inevitably left behind many accounts in history.

Moreover, there were the flower thieves on the mountains, who hunted floral and botanical spirits to refine them into pills. Twelve small flower pills could be made from capturing one hundred and eight floral spirits, resulting in a large pill. Their methods were extremely vicious, yet their effects were astonishing, making them formidable enemies to the Hundred Flowers Blessed Land. It’s said that the founder of this flower-thieving lineage had a hidden grudge against the lord of the Hundred Flowers Blessed Land.

Many seemingly righteous celestial masters who publicly eradicated such practices often secretly accepted them as their supporters, opening up vast streams of revenue.

Upon hearing this, Chen Ping'an curiously asked, "Are the goddesses of the Hundred Flowers Blessed Land truly ancient floral spirits among them?"

He recalled the murals on the Bone Beach.

Lianxin nodded, "I once captured a flower thief at the Nascent Soul level and brought them to the Hundred Flowers Blessed Land, exchanging them for a crucial treasure. It's certain that the four flower gods are indeed ancient, while the lord of the blessed land belongs to the later generations."

At this point, Lianxin glanced at the young man, "Thanks to the poetic verses of scholars."

Chen Ping'an smiled, "Writing poetry has never been my strong suit; it seems I am destined to have no connection with the Hundred Flowers Blessed Land."

Lianxin remarked, "Are you sure you can return alive to the Hao Ran realm?"

Chen Ping'an replied, "I will strive for that."
