Except for the fact that Li Cai was resolutely determined to thrust out her next sword, even at the cost of her life.

In the distance, a young woman was arriving on her sword, her aura formidable.

It was the one named Ning Yao.

Without warning, the old man shattered his life sword, closing his eyes with a light laugh, “Though I have yet to draw a sword, I die with purpose.”

Clouds and mist enveloped the area.

Yao Chongdao, employing his soul and sword intent combined with his life sword, crafted a world.

The next moment, Huang Luan found herself enveloped in dense white mist.

A celestial sword immortal, wielding a flying sword that was not a life-bound divine spell but had the means to bind a great demon—what significance did that hold?

Who could kill me? 

Li Cai? Or that Ning Yao, who was ultimately only in the Nascent Soul realm?

In the far distance, a certain scoundrel was beating two great demons, vanishing into thin air, directly breaking through two imposing small worlds.

One was a towering giant with three heads and six arms, his stance always accompanied by a golden cushion.

He had once been the first to ascend the Sword Qi Great Wall, only to be cleaved down by Chen Qingdu, after which he deliberately left a deep sword scar.

The other was a diminutive old man wielding a long staff, arriving atop the giant's shoulders, puzzled, “How strange?”

Moments later, within a battlefield, the clouds dispersed, revealing the truth.

A man, wielding Yao Chongdao's “Lian Yun” sword, pierced a great demon's head, lifting it high, and indifferently declared, “The slayer of Huang Luan is Yao Chongdao, A Liang.”

On the great moon that served as the battlefield, a tall old sword immortal stood atop a massive demon corpse, laughing heartily, “A Liang, how is it?!”

The sword severed the Lotus Blossom Temple's master—only Dong Sangeng alone.

Having discarded his life sword, the old man could still return to the Sword Qi Great Wall, exploding his sword intent to envelop the entire great moon, then manifesting a massive Dharma form to drag the great moon down to the earth, smashing it into the heavily gathered ranks of the Wildlands demons.

The great moon began to shatter, and the old sword immortal's figure gradually dissipated.

As the great moon descended, its overwhelming force compelled Yang Zhi, Fiery Concubine, and four other great demons to face that old sword immortal named Dong.

A Liang raised his arm high, giving a thumbs up.

*(End of Chapter)*

 **Chapter 800: The Moon in the Sky (Part One)**

Nianxin was furious. "Chen Ping'an, what’s going on?!"

Sitting beside her, Shuangjiang let out a gentle sigh. One couldn't really blame the girl for her temper; she had grown accustomed to the tenacious nature of the Hidden Official Ancestor. In the past, every time they had sewn, they had persevered through countless accidents, so the seamstress had become used to the unexpected. No matter how dangerous the process was, it seemed they always managed to succeed. This time, however, the unexpected was truly unexpected.

After slaying another Yuanying realm demon sword cultivator within this cage, Nianxin needed to inscribe the true name of an ancient, ferocious beast during today’s sewing. She had to pierce through Chen Ping'an's back with her life-bound embroidery needle, connecting to his spine. With only two strokes left to finish, they were still short of success. If Nianxin hadn’t withdrawn her knife in time, Chen Ping'an's entire spine would have snapped in two, and the residual aura of the great demon's true name would have surged into his heart like a tidal wave of malevolence. If it weren't for the remnants of a few golden talisman texts still lingering in Chen Ping'an's mind, which Nianxin was quite familiar with, she would have had no way to suppress the malevolent aura. Consequently, Chen Ping'an's body and soul might have been reduced to a series of exploding firecrackers, with an ending akin to a celestial being self-destructing their golden core or Yuanying—impossible for even a deity to save.

The young Hidden Official lay on the ground, unable to rise. His back was flayed open, exposing his spine. Curled up on the floor, he twitched uncontrollably, blood pooling around him, mingling with the remnants of the great demon's true name lingering in the blood. In the end, the concentrated malevolence coalesced into a tiny "golden core" of sorts, hoping to become a descending spirit through the blood. If this were in the vast realm of righteousness, neglecting to control it might lead to the birth of a true golden core specter. If it found a sufficiently malevolent ancient battlefield, it could gather ghostly soldiers, establish a netherworld residence, and erect a king's banner, becoming a demon king that wreaks havoc for miles.

Nianxin was in a similar state of misery, vomiting several mouthfuls of pitch-black blood, this time not forcing it back down, but turning to spit on the ground.

The foreign demon of the Erqing serpent waved its robe's sleeve and extracted the swiftly forming true name spirit from the blood-soaked ground, suspending it before them. Shuangjiang extended her fingers and gently crushed it. The filth and malevolence that could have turned a lower-level Yuanying cultivator into a spirit puppet dissipated completely.

Moments later, Chen Ping'an managed to sit up. His soul trembled, and his body convulsed as if a giant fish were flipping beneath the ground. His blood boiled as if a flood were raging within, thankfully, his life-bound objects began to circulate on their own, helping to calm the anomalies, allowing Chen Ping'an to maintain the steadiness of his fleshly body. He apologetically said, "I really can't take it anymore."

Shuangjiang shot a meaningful glance at Nianxin, signaling her to stop rubbing salt in the wound.

Though Nianxin ceased her tirade, her expression remained displeased as she said in a low voice, "We're about to strike at Yunqing and Qingqiu. If you continue like this, I suggest you just stop. After all, this true name 'garment' is barely usable now."

Chen Ping'an nodded.

After Nianxin helped Chen Ping'an roughly stitch up his wounds, she vanished in an instant.

Her seemingly "careless" actions of adding the final touches were all part of a tacit understanding among the three: Nianxin pretended to be clumsy, Chen Ping'an acted as though he was oblivious, and Shuangjiang feigned ignorance.

Once Nianxin left, Shuangjiang cautiously advised, "Hidden Official Ancestor, each time you exchange your life for another's, your physical condition deteriorates. It's already difficult enough, and then you immediately have to deal with stitching? This is not a wise course of action."

If she didn't proceed with the sewing, Chen Ping'an's body and divine consciousness would recover rapidly, like a sickly person who has just regained their health, or someone who has been blind for ages finally seeing light. He would be immersed in a relaxing, comfortable "little world." At this moment, he could already stumble to his feet, his form slightly hunched as he took slow steps, the large pool of blood on the ground having been cleared away by Shuangjiang, and the remnants of the true name demon had long been collected by Nianxin into her embroidery bag. Shuangjiang silently praised the diligent seamstress, who was quite the clever girl.

Chen Ping'an said, "Right now, sewing is just too painful. Every time I kill a demon, the thought of it makes my heart tremble. I just want to finish it all in one go. Besides, Nianxin said that the more pain I endure, the deeper the memory, the better the effect."

Shuangjiang slowly replied, "With the cage's suppression, every time you decide to exchange lives at a critical moment, a place of impossibility is quietly forged, and all your methods come into play. That's how you've narrowly managed to slay Yuanying sword cultivators time and time again. Just like that cockroach-like sword cultivator, even after being suppressed by you to a half-step down in realm, it still managed to stab your heart with one blow. If it were anyone else, taking that 'merciless' strike would mean certain death."

"And how would you kill the others in the upper five realms? Mengpo and Qingqiu are slightly easier; Mengpo's life-bound divine ability is proficient in illusion, which doesn't affect you much. Just give her a loophole to exploit. Qingqiu is naturally at a disadvantage due to being slain by you. The bamboo's life-bound painting struggles to unfold fully within the cage's little world. If it spreads the painting, you fold the mountains and rivers, each countering the other; there's bound to be some opportunity. But that Yunqing is a different story. These four are just discussing whether you have any chance at all. As for the immortal realm Lord Changjun, you have no hope whatsoever. The moment you open the cage door, it's a death sentence."

Shuangjiang concluded, "Unless... unless you reach the pinnacle of the martial artist realm, simultaneously breaking through the Guanghai and Longmen realms as a Qi practitioner, enabling you to ascend to the golden core. Of course, the premise is to avoid provoking that Lord Changjun, as the realm disparity is too great; no amount of scheming would be of any use."

Chen Ping'an stepped out of the prison. "The pinnacle of the martial artist realm, attaining the golden core? You make it sound easy. You have no idea what my current situation and plans are."

The foreign demon, following closely behind, repeatedly clenched its fists, arms lifting above its head, shouting, “The Ancestor handles matters without discrimination of size, lifting heavy things as if they were light. A thousand-pound task is like a feather, and endless worries are but a drizzle. The Ancestor can turn clouds and rain with a single hand...”

As a result, it took a punch from the not-so-pleased Chen Ping'an, shattering its form. After reassembling, it appeared listless and no longer noisy.

Being a loyal but stubborn minister, untrusted, while being a treacherous sycophant also earns you a beating. Truly, the intentions of heaven are hard to fathom; accompanying a ruler is like being with a tiger.

Chen Ping'an walked toward the pavilion below the prison.

The five Yuanying sword cultivator demons, including the yellow-brown one, followed the general path that Shuangjiang had outlined. The sole goal was to leverage their timing and advantages to surpass the Yuanying sword cultivators. Thus, it didn’t count as a pure sword duel among sword cultivators, nor could it be deemed unfair. The yellow-brown ones, as sword cultivators, also possessed their own secret techniques and hidden skills. Chen Ping'an's greatest reliance was still on his life-bound object, the cage of the sparrow, and its little world. The cultivation realms of both sides were evenly matched, and he would additionally have the advantage of the martial artist's supernatural power.

According to Shuangjiang, as long as Chen Ping'an eventually reached the Yupu realm, nurturing the Cage of the Sparrow properly, then the future "mutual rise and fall" would mean each side was at one realm's disparity; if you fell a realm while I rose a realm, that would be the true demeanor of a sword immortal. Breaking through realms to slay enemies would be as easy as picking up coins off the ground.

However, these were all distant, unreachable matters—something to ponder and derive joy from for now.

Upon reaching the pavilion, Chen Ping'an sat cross-legged, laying the narrow blade of "Zhan Kan" across his knees. He began his breathing exercises to refine his residual martial luck while also contemplating the deal with Shuangjiang, multitasking by practicing and discussing both matters.

After ascending to the Dongfu realm, regardless of how Shuangjiang, who was in the Ascending realm, viewed it, for Chen Ping'an himself, accustomed to the ups and downs of the lower five realm cultivators, returning to cultivate as a mid-five realm immortal was a world of difference.

As he breathed in a leisurely manner, a misty white aura filled the air around his facial orifices, pure spiritual energy swirling like slender yet striking white serpents hanging from a cliff.

Particularly at the center of his brow, a particle of innate spiritual light flickered between brightness and dimness.

And at the corners of his eyes, golden light flowed faintly, his eyes resembling two chambers, with two bright lamps illuminating the bamboo curtains at the entrance.

This was the “earthly immortal, the appearance of enlightenment” that Qi practitioners below the Earth Immortal realm dream of.

Fighting against five Yuanying sword cultivators, whether honing his martial arts to forcibly temper his martial luck into the mountain roots of his bones, or examining his injuries to patch up his weaknesses, even refining the flaws of his life-bound object, the gains could be described as immense.

Shuangjiang adhered to the rules, not stepping even half a foot into the pavilion, like a wandering ghost drifting outside.

Chen Ping'an's agreement with the foreign demon about a grain of Gu Yu coin was nearing its conclusion.

A grain of Gu Yu coin could be divided into ten small Summer Solstice coins, all of which were Shuangjiang's life-saving money.

Having gifted the execution object from the ancient Dragon-slaying Platform, the narrow blade "Zhan Kan," Shuangjiang received the first Summer Solstice coin, a fortunate start.

The series of inscriptions containing "The Clear Heart" could assist Chen Ping'an, during his seated meditation and breathing exercises, to forget his physical form more quickly, allowing his mind to delve deeper. The effect was akin to a Daoist's sitting on a celestial mat or lighting incense in a cave. Although it belonged to the slow and steady method, it was by no means negligible. Lower five realm cultivators drawing upon the spiritual energy of heaven and earth were like cupping water with both hands—very arduous; while upon reaching the mid-five realm, it was akin to using a bucket to draw from a well—naturally much faster.

Not only did Chen Ping'an acquire a treasure blade that could suppress the likes of dragons, but he also gained lasting benefits for his future cultivation, a great deal.

For the second Summer Solstice coin, Chen Ping'an had Shuangjiang elaborate on the cultivation techniques for the Dongfu, Guanghai, and Longmen realms, including all the combinations for refining life-bound objects of various levels.

Chen Ping'an decided to ascend to the Dongfu realm within the prison, as Shuangjiang confidently stated, this opportunity was one that would be lost if missed. Utilizing this chance to roam within, she assisted in locating six of the ten mountains that had already opened up their life-bound apertures, successfully obtaining the third Summer Solstice coin.

While Shuangjiang taught and clarified the Dao, she also managed to strike an additional deal with her abilities. She mentioned the banner of the sword immortal that had been refined in the mid-levels. It needed to be placed atop the mountain shrine using secret techniques. At that time, she had not discussed the details, so Chen Ping'an willingly took the bait. The foreign demon earned its share, while the Hidden Official Ancestor, a Dongfu realm Qi practitioner, gained another cultivation technique, adding to his skills.

Furthermore, she explained how to refine the mock White Jade Capital Tower into a new aperture in the Guanghai realm after refining it into a life-bound object. It could serve as an important auxiliary life-bound object, absorbing the spiritual energy of heaven and earth. The five elements that naturally breed within a person's little world could be refined in this "White Jade Capital," yielding twice the result with half the effort, fostering five life-bound objects. This was Shuangjiang's timely assistance.

In addition, she provided methods to add finishing touches to the wall paintings of the Water Palace. The three types of celestial techniques Shuangjiang imparted to the Hidden Official Ancestor cost Chen Ping'an only one Summer Solstice coin.

At this point, Shuangjiang had already secured four Summer Solstice coins.

The two short swords, seemingly casually mentioned by Shuangjiang as "the boat carving from years past," were deliberately left vague, concealing their true origin. One bore the inscription "Dirt," and the other "Lake." The former had already been placed within Chen Ping'an's sword nurturing gourd and didn't count as a trade, but the "Lake" sword, which Shuangjiang claimed was better when paired, was priced at one Summer Solstice coin, and Chen Ping'an agreed.

Unbeknownst to him, the foreign demon had already earned five Summer Solstice coins.

Once Chen Ping'an reached the Longmen realm, he could begin to refine the two ancient relic swords into the water dragons of the Water Palace. As for the originally water-dan coalesced water luck dragon, it would be refined into a pearl of water luck. In the future, the denser the water luck became, the higher the grade of that pearl would be.

Initially gifting a "Dirt" sword, followed by discussing the benefits of refining the "Lake" sword, along with the banner of the sword immortal and the mock White Jade Capital, were all part of the foreign demon's fishing strategy, offering half the bait and keeping the other half.

Chen Ping'an had no objection to Shuangjiang's business methods; after all, it was a fair trade and not forced selling.

In addition, Shuangjiang had gradually used her true and false celestial robe, the two green serpents hanging from her ears, and all the gold and fragments of the golden body she had earned in a fifty-fifty split with "Long Life," to strike four more Summer Solstice coin deals with Chen Ping'an.

Only one Summer Solstice coin remained.

Gathering enough for a grain of Gu Yu coin, according to their agreement, the foreign demon Shuangjiang would be able to leave the prison immediately, gaining a sense of carefree freedom. Moreover, once she left the prison, neither Chen Ping'an nor Chen Qingdu could target her in any way. As long as she did not follow the demon clan into the vast realm of righteousness or harm any sword cultivator of the Sword Qi Great Wall, she could choose to become a local tyrant in the wilderness or hide in the vast realm of righteousness, establishing a sect at her whim.

During this time, Shuangjiang had previously agreed to owe a snowflake coin, buying a little story from Chen Ping'an.

In turn, Chen Ping'an quickly used a snowflake coin to trade for the true material of that Five Thunder Stamp.

Shuangjiang suddenly said, "I thought that seemingly inconspicuous snowflake coin would determine the outcome of our deal. I didn't expect you to eliminate my doubts so quickly."

Once Shuangjiang secured nine Summer Solstice coins, plus a bunch of miscellaneous snowflake coins, even if she was only short one snowflake coin of a grain of Gu Yu coin, the deal would still not be fulfilled.

The awkwardness of this transaction for Shuangjiang, the foreign demon, lay in the fact that she was just one Summer Solstice coin short—it was a dead end. Even if she were short just a snowflake coin, it would still be a dead end.

Chen Ping'an remained with his eyes closed, candidly stating, "At first, I did consider playing tricks with that snowflake coin, but I changed my mind later."

Shuangjiang halted, anxiously asking, "You’re not planning to withhold the last Summer Solstice coin from me, are you? Hidden Official Ancestor, please don’t conduct business like that; it’s too hurtful."

Chen Ping'an opened his eyes and shook his head. "Of course not. The matter regarding the first Summer Solstice coin means you can live."

Shuangjiang gently nodded, confused, "I know this, but I’ve never dared to believe it."

Chen Ping'an said, "Do you really want to see Shuangjiang again? For a foreign demon that has gained pure freedom, do you still need such an obsession?"

A moment of silence ensued as Chen Ping'an continued, "You are no longer merely a celestial couple. Besides, with your cultivation and mindset, when and where would you not be with that great cultivator Shuangjiang, inseparable?"

Because Shuangjiang's heart demon was the woman he loved.

It should be after Shuangjiang ascended to the upper five realms that this connection arose and persisted until Shuangjiang reached the Ascending realm. It was even possible that it was during her attempts to reach the lost realms that this foreign demon truly materialized. However, Shuangjiang never managed to completely sever this heart demon, ultimately leading to their separation. It was likely that Shuangjiang had utilized some profound Daoist technique to merely expel the heart demon but was never able to truly subdue or refine it. Yet, these were all just unsubstantiated speculations; the truth of the matter was known only to heaven, unless Chen Ping'an were to visit the Qingming realm in the future and meet the true "Shuangjiang."

The foreign demon squinted, asking, "How did you guess that? Was it the embroidered handkerchief from that woman's boudoir that revealed my background, or did my instinct evade you when you touched my head?"

Chen Ping'an retorted, "What guessing? Wasn’t it you who wanted me to know the truth?"

The white-haired boyish foreign demon chuckled, hovering in the air, clapping gently. "What a Hidden Official Ancestor! You never fail to disappoint me, Chen Ping'an."

Chen Ping'an declared, "For the last Summer Solstice coin, let’s make a hundred-year agreement: before we reunite, you help me protect someone in secret."

The white-haired boy lightly flicked the ear of the green serpent, saying, "In the fifth realm, only Qi practitioners below the upper five realms are allowed to enter. I can’t go against Confucian rules. I’m powerless here; this deal is difficult for me. Chen Ping'an, that’s not fair; you’re intentionally making it hard for me."

Chen Ping'an shook his head. "My teacher is over there, and I believe the Confucian sage guarding the passage will eventually turn a blind eye. But you only have one chance to act; after that, at most, you’ll be expelled by the Confucian sage. At that point, you'll follow my teacher's arrangements for retreat. Whether it's returning to the vast realm of righteousness, settling on Falling Star Mountain, or being imprisoned in the Merit Forest, I will find you, no matter what it costs, and I will uphold my promise to restore your freedom. If you don't act, we’ll meet in the fifth realm."

The white-haired boy queried, "What if?"

Chen Ping'an replied solemnly, "What if I cannot keep my promise to find you? Regardless, after a hundred years, you will still obtain your freedom."

The white-haired boy began to wander around the pavilion, seemingly weighing the pros and cons.

He started discussing details with the young Hidden Official, "Scholars value face. If I swagger about hidden within the soul of some sword cultivator, that can't be considered hidden. Even if your teacher helps soften the blow, that won't be appropriate. If Nianxin could enter the fifth realm, her soul is profound enough, but she's in the Yupu realm and cannot go. This cannot be blamed on me; that great demon from the Capturing and Releasing Pavilion, first, its skills are specialized, plus it can hide within the depths of a golden core sword cultivator's mind, successfully evading all the sword immortals. Clearly, this is not something that can be accomplished overnight. If you give me three to five years to grind it out, I can find a golden core cultivator to take root."

Chen Ping'an said, "I will help you find a hidden place."

The white-haired boy mused, "Hidden Official Ancestor, you’ve planned everything. No matter how many words I have in my heart, they seem to evaporate when they reach my lips."

Chen Ping'an stood up, re-attaching the Zhan Kan to his waist. "If you agree to this, I ask you, in that new realm, not to do anything unnecessary. No more 'let’s see.' Otherwise, you will have to burn incense every day, praying for my demise on the Sword Qi Great Wall."

Chen Ping'an laughed, squinting, "In the past, before every fight, I never liked to speak harshly to others. Today, I’m making an exception for you; please cherish it."

The white-haired boy no longer wore a cheeky smile but bowed respectfully, "I will heed the Ancestor's decree. Starting now, the deal for a grain of Gu Yu coin is settled."

Chen Ping'an leaned back and fell to the ground, his hands cradling the back of his head. "I’ll first see how Meng Po and Qing Qiu are faring. If I can’t handle them, then I’ll have to rely on you to act on my behalf with your celestial methods."

Chen Ping'an closed his eyes, saying, "Perhaps you intentionally let me know the identity of the woman, mistakenly believing that you are the heart demon that Shuangjiang cares for. In truth, it’s all a ruse; it doesn’t matter. You’ve won; after all, I’ve lost nothing."

The white-haired boy's expression grew despondent. "To carry a hero's burden without freedom, seeing the Hidden Official Ancestor like this truly tugs at the heartstrings."

Chen Ping'an drew his sword from its sheath without glancing at the foreign demon, swiftly striking down. The foreign demon quickly reassembled, hopping toward the pavilion, giving a thumbs-up repeatedly, alternating hands. "Not every hero can sway the heavens, nor are they all capable of causing the mountains and rivers to sink. Ancestor... oh, what a superb sword technique!"

Nianxin sat on the distant steps, watching the foreign demon and the azure-clad guest in the pavilion. As parting drew near, she felt an unexpected pang of reluctance. 

In her life as a seamstress, she had never encountered such lively yet peaceful times; she no longer had to worry about the unexpected schemes on the mountains, nor did she see eyes looking at her as if she were a ghost.

The trio walked down a desolate street. Li Cai donned a snow-white robe, with a slender white sword, "Frost Jiao," hanging at her waist, its blade already snapped in two.

Along with this woman, the leader of the Floating Sea Sword Sect, were the youth Chen Li and the girl Gao Youqing, who would follow Li Cai to North Julu Prefecture as her direct disciples.

Li Cai believed she was not as heroic as the likes of Lu Zhi; her appearance had returned to normal, the scars on her face were not obvious, although her complexion was pale, clearly not fully healed from her severe injuries. The true hidden danger lay within her life-bound flying sword, Snowflake, which had suffered extensive damage. It was likely she would never reach the immortal realm in this lifetime. However, Li Cai didn’t mind; a woman with a high realm often struggled to find a husband, no matter how good her temper was.

After arriving at the Sword Qi Great Wall, this female sword immortal had engaged in continuous battles, leading the charge each time. In the past few years, the rules of the Summer Palace had been many, and the Hidden Official's flying sword was the most troublesome, imposing heavier restrictions on sword immortals. Among many sword cultivators, she had likely scolded the young Hidden Official the most vigorously, far surpassing local sword cultivators.

After being severely injured and retreating from the city wall, she abandoned all her war merits, seeking only a long sword from the sword shop and a robe from the clothing shop.

A close friend, the Great Immortal Li Yu, had once promised to join her in going to the Sword Qi Great Wall to slay demons.

Upon reaching the tavern, Li Cai scrutinized the "no business" sign, finally tearing down a piece from the wall and holding it in her hand.

Not in a hurry to return to North Julu Prefecture, she planned to travel to South Poso Prefecture, perhaps to visit the mountain peak of the sword immortal Yuan Qingshu.

Li Cai carried with her a battered sword nurturing gourd, a relic of Yuan Qingshu, which should also be returned to his sect.

Years ago, on the city wall, Yuan Qingshu had joked with the local sword immortal Gao Kui, using the sword nurturing gourd as a wine vessel, pairing it with the name of a great demon for an exquisite taste.

In the end, both had perished.

Li Cai turned to the two small heads at the tavern's entrance, smiling, "Tell the second shopkeeper that this 'no business' sign has been taken by Li Cai."

Feng Kangle responded, "What does it matter? Just take it. A woman as beautiful as you, if the second shopkeeper sees you, he wouldn’t dare utter a word."

It was one thing to spend money drinking at another shop, but to cause a ruckus here would only humiliate their own tavern.

Tao Ban, with a good memory, recalled all the customers who bought and drank at the tavern, asking, "Sister Li, why hasn’t the second shopkeeper shown his face? Has he covered his face again, dressing himself up, secretly slaying demons?"

Li Cai laughed, "Sister Li? Did the second shopkeeper teach you that?"

Tao Ban nodded.

Feng Kangle complained, "Why did you act so foolishly? You lost all your sincerity in an instant."

Li Cai restrained her smile, saying, "Bring me one jar of every type of liquor; I want to take it to South Poso Prefecture."

Gao Youqing was engraving words onto the "no business" sign with her flying sword when Chen Li remarked, "What’s so good about that Pang Yuanji?"

Gao Youqing turned, hiding the sign, and retorted in anger, "That’s none of your business."

Li Cai stood at the threshold of the tavern, gazing at the city wall.

She had come here to wield her sword freely, not realizing that her swordsmanship was far from sufficient, ultimately accruing a tremendous debt of gratitude to that Yao sword immortal. The crucial question was how she would repay it in the future.

The youth looked dejected. "Master, does that mean I will be a disciple of the Floating Sea Sword Sect from now on?"

Li Cai said, "Then learn from this second shopkeeper. 'In the vast realm of righteousness, Hidden Official Chen Ping'an. At the Sword Qi Great Wall, Floating Sea Sword Lake Chen Li. Both do not interfere with each other. The hometown is always ahead, while the identity of a cultivator comes after, not forgetting one's roots.'"

The youth nodded, it was a viable plan.

Ultimately, Li Cai led the youth and girl away from the Sword Qi Great Wall.

The Upside Down Mountain temporarily had no ferry service to North Julu Prefecture, so they randomly found a celestial inn to stay in.

Li Cai drank alone.

Li Tui Mi, Tao Wen, Zhou Cheng, Nalan Yexing, Gao Kui, Yao Chongdao, Dong Sangeng...

The young sword cultivators, many of whom were of similar ages to Chen Li and Gao Youqing, would only continue to increase in number.

Li Cai’s vision blurred with drink, leaning against the window. "Damn this broken Yupu realm."

Gao Youqing was staying next door, still adjusting to the vastly different environment between Upside Down Mountain and the Sword Qi Great Wall, where the spiritual energy and sword energy differed greatly.

Chen Li, carefree, while practicing his sword, weighed his purse at a store in the inn that specialized in selling mountain treasures. The entire Spirit Herb Lodge had already relocated. Previously clearing stock, they had sold many low-quality miscellaneous spiritual artifacts at a bargain to various familiar forces of Upside Down Mountain, this inn was one of them, so although there were not many treasures, at first glance, it was still dazzling.

Li Cai, always paying attention to Chen Li's sword intent from afar, furrowed her brow. Her murderous intent surged, and she dashed off.

Li Cai seized the youth's life-bound flying sword, blood flowing from her palm and dripping onto the floor, utterly unaware, saying to Chen Li, "So many sword cultivators have died; it’s not for you to come to the vast realm of righteousness to seek death. If you truly want to die, wait until you become a sword immortal. Killing a Guanghai realm sword cultivator, who would remember who you are? If you keep this up, you might as well become a wild cultivator in the mountains; you would surely die quickly. Otherwise, in your future cultivation, you get killed first, and I’ll be so furious I won’t know how to avenge you."

The person targeted by Chen Li's flying sword was a shopkeeper who appeared panicked. Upon seeing Li Cai, he bowed deeply in apology, offering numerous justifications, claiming ignorance and pleading not to die. After all, it was mainly Chen Li's unstable heart and excessive murderous intent that had caused this situation; he had already left the battlefield, but his heart was still reverberating there.

This was a good thing, but if Li Cai continued to ignore it, then even if Chen Li reached North Julu Prefecture, as long as he went down the mountain to explore, he would die.

Li Cai opened her hand, and the youth immediately retracted his flying sword.

Chen Li said apologetically, "I harbor no resentment towards my master or North Julu Prefecture."

Li Cai smiled, "Master doesn’t care about that. All I care about is whether you’ve practiced your sword diligently and if the Floating Sea Sword Lake can really produce a sword immortal in a hundred years."

Chen Li honestly replied, "Reaching sword immortal status within a hundred years is somewhat challenging."

Li Cai patted the youth's shoulder, wiping the blood from her palm. "You’re a big man; show some spirit! As my direct disciple, even if you’re only a mid-five realm sword cultivator, when speaking with others, especially when calling for battles, you should carry yourself with the demeanor of an upper-five realm sword immortal!"

Hearing the terms "centenarian sword immortal" and "hundred-year sword immortal," the shopkeeper in charge of the tavern trembled violently, regretting his actions and quickly thinking of ways to remedy the situation.

Li Cai and the youth exchanged heartfelt words, so the youth reluctantly "bought" the intriguing spirit artifact at a high price.

On their way back to their lodgings, Li Cai asked, "Do you remember that guy? Find a way to get your own revenge in the future."

Chen Li's face brightened as he nodded vigorously.

Li Cai knocked on Gao Youqing's door, grabbing the girl's face and twisting it, "Chen Li needs to keep his temper in check! Gao Youqing, what’s wrong with you? Are you too timid and afraid of trouble? When Chen Li draws his sword, Master will stop him, but he’ll be happy in his heart. You, on the other hand, just stand there and watch the excitement from afar, showing no intention to draw your sword? That makes Master very unhappy!"

Gao Youqing, still being pinched, nervously said, "Master, my brother told me to endure and not provoke trouble once I arrive at the vast realm of righteousness."

Li Cai spat, "No wonder Gao Ye is still a pitiful Yuanying."

Gao Youqing's eyes turned red instantly. 

It wasn’t just the yearning for her brother, who had been her companion since childhood, but also the worry that their separation wasn't just simple, but rather a silent farewell.

Li Cai immediately released her grip, gently saying, "Alright, alright. Endure if you must, but Master can teach you both a clever little trick. If you’re bullied, just endure it, but if a fellow disciple is bullied, you must chop that person to the ground! Kill the ones that need killing, and if not, just give them a good beating! Our Floating Sea Sword Lake has some resources; we can afford their medical expenses! That way, both you and Chen Li can endure when you need to, and release your frustrations when it's time. If it comes down to a fight, just return home and call Master to step in again..."

Initially, the youth and girl found this amusing, but upon hearing "return home," they both fell silent and dejected.

Li Cai sighed lightly, waved her hand, and went off to drink, leaving her disciples with a simple instruction: "Go practice your swords."

The old deaf man finally returned to the prison, accompanied by Youyu and Changming, for the first time visiting that pavilion.

The prison where Mengpo resided was already empty.

The old deaf man caught a glimpse of the young Hidden Official, clad in unfamiliar robes that were oversized and trailing on the ground.

Chen Ping'an seemed to be in a meditative state, completely oblivious to the arrival of the old deaf man.

The old deaf man reached out and grabbed the jade hairpin that Chen Ping'an had tucked in his hair, drawing it toward himself, saying in a deep voice, "The sword immortal needs this for a moment, it will be returned to the Hidden Official shortly."

Chen Ping'an remained unmoved.

The old deaf man glanced at Nianxin, who was sitting at the bottom of the steps, carefully stowing the jade hairpin into his sleeve. He didn’t trust that foreign demon, but this stubborn little girl was still more reliable.

Nianxin sensed the old deaf man’s scrutinizing gaze and spoke up, "It’s fine; he brought it upon himself. It has nothing to do with Wu Shuangjiang."

The woman who manifested from the golden copper coins slightly frowned.

Shuangjiang smiled, "Long Life Dao friend, in this world of business, there’s no such thing as taking all the advantages. You must give back nine for every ten received; that’s the truth. You should learn from my ancestor a bit."

The woman nodded gently.

Youyu, for some reason, looked at the young Hidden Official's figure at that moment and felt a twinge of fear.

The old deaf man hurriedly left, vanishing from the prison.

The youth and woman ascended the steps together.

Shuangjiang followed behind, saying, "Long Life Dao friend, shall we continue to scour the land?"

The woman smiled, "I have been waiting eagerly."

Gao Kui, with his last sword strike, questioned the sword master, Dragon Lord.

After receiving the sword, Dragon Lord personally slain the last sword immortal of the sect.

Not far from the gray-robed figure, the skeletal white Ying sat on the throne, watching this scene, feeling that the minds of these sword cultivators were truly baffling.

(End of chapter)

 **Chapter 800: The Moon in the Sky (Part One)**

Niangxin was furious, "Chen Ping'an, what’s the matter with you?!"

Sitting beside them, Shuangjiang let out a gentle sigh. It was hard to blame the young girl for her fiery temper; she had grown accustomed to the firmness of the Hidden Official’s disposition. Previously, every time they sewed, they managed to endure, so it became second nature for the seamstress to expect both minor and major mishaps. Regardless of how dangerous the process seemed, success always felt inevitable. But this time, the unexpected was indeed very unexpected.

Within this cage, after slaying yet another Yuan Ying realm demon sword cultivator, Niangxin needed to engrave the true name of an ancient ferocious beast onto Chen Ping'an's back this time during their sewing. She had to pierce through with her life-bound needle and connect to his spine, and with only two strokes remaining, it was still a near failure. If Niangxin hadn’t sheathed her knife in time, Chen Ping'an's entire spine would have snapped in two, and the residual aura of the ferocious beast's true name would have surged like a tidal wave into his heart. If it weren’t for a few leftover words from the Golden Jade Codex in Chen Ping'an’s mind that Niangxin was familiar with, quickly used to suppress the aura of the true name, he might have ended up as nothing more than a series of exploding firecrackers, much like that earth immortal who self-destructed their golden core and Yuan Ying—no divine being could save him then.

The young Hidden Official lay on the ground, unable to rise, his back flayed open, exposing his spine. His body curled on the ground, twitching, blood pooling around him, mingling with the lingering malevolence of the demon’s true name. In the end, the thick residual malice coalesced into a grain-sized "golden core," aiming to use his blood as its "foundation for cultivation," hoping to become a descending spirit. If they were in the vast world of righteousness, without intervention, perhaps in an instant, a genuine golden core ghost would arise, finding a sufficiently malevolent ancient battlefield to gather ghostly soldiers, build a netherworld dwelling, and establish a king's banner, thus becoming a calamity-spawning ghost king.

Niangxin, too, was in a sorry state, spitting out several mouthfuls of dark, ink-like blood, this time not forcing it back down but turning her head to spit it on the ground.

The Outer Heavenly Demon of the Qing Snake waved its robe sleeve casually, pulling the quickly forming grain-sized spirit of the true name from the pool of blood on the ground, suspending it before them. Shuangjiang stretched out her fingers, gently crushing it. Those vile malevolent energies, sufficient to turn a lower five realms cultivator into an undead puppet, vanished without a trace.

Moments later, Chen Ping'an sat up, his soul trembling, his internal muscles and bones vibrating slightly, as if a light-scaled fish was flipping beneath the ground. His blood boiled like floods raging everywhere. Fortunately, the five elemental life-bound items began to operate on their own, helping to calm the anomalies, allowing Chen Ping'an to maintain his physical form, apologizing, "I really can't take it anymore."

Shuangjiang shot a look at Niangxin, signaling her not to rub salt into the wounds anymore.

Though Niangxin stopped cursing, her expression remained displeased as she spoke in a low voice, "We’ll be going after Yunqing and Qingqiu soon. If you’re still this useless, I suggest you just stop here. After all, this true name 'garment' is barely usable now."

Chen Ping'an nodded.

After Niangxin helped Chen Ping'an patch his skin roughly, she vanished in a flash.

Her few "unintentional" embellishments were deliberately overlooked, with Chen Ping'an pretending to ignore them and Shuangjiang pretending not to see. The three shared an unspoken understanding.

Once Niangxin left, Shuangjiang cautiously persuaded, "Hidden Official, every time you use your life to exchange for another, your body is left on the brink. It’s already difficult enough; you shouldn’t immediately sew after slaying a demon. This is not wise."

If he didn’t sew, Chen Ping'an’s body and spirit would recover quickly, like a sick person just recovering from a severe illness, or like someone who had been blind for a long time finally seeing the light. He would be immersed in a relaxed and comfortable "little world." At this moment, Chen Ping'an could already stumble to his feet, his figure hunched, slowly wandering about. The large pool of blood on the ground had long been cleaned up after Shuangjiang dispelled the true name’s evil spirit, and it had been neatly stored away by Niangxin in her embroidery pouch. Shuangjiang quietly praised how diligent and frugal the seamstress was, and how she had turned the tables on the young lady.

Chen Ping'an said, "Now, the sewing part is just too painful. Every time I think about killing a demon, I tremble at the thought and want to get it done in one go. Moreover, Niangxin has said that the more it hurts, the more profound the memory, and the better the effect."

Shuangjiang slowly replied, "With the confinement of the caged bird, each time you decide to exchange your life, a place is subtly crafted where none can intervene. Every time, you narrowly manage to slay a Yuan Ying sword cultivator, just like that cockroach-like sword cultivator you suppressed by half a realm—how could that not result in him striking your heart with a single sword? If it were anyone else, after being hit by that 'savage' sword, they would be dead for sure."

"How would you kill the others in the upper five realms? Meng Po and Qingqiu are somewhat manageable; Meng Po’s life-bound divine ability specializes in illusions, which doesn’t affect you much—just give her a flaw to exploit. Qingqiu, on the other hand, is naturally hindered by the sword's suppression. The bamboo shoot's life-bound painting, within the caged bird’s little world, the bamboo shoot’s divine ability is hard to fully unleash. When the bamboo shoot spreads the painting, you can fold mountains and rivers, and it’s still possible to seize an opportunity. But Yunqing? That’s a different story. These four are merely discussing whether you have the slightest chance. As for the immortal realm’s Hou Changjun, you have no chance at all; once the prison door opens, it’s a death sentence."

Shuangjiang concluded, "Unless… unless you reach the peak of the Martial Husband realm and simultaneously break through the Observing Sea and Dragon Gate realms to reach the Golden Core. The premise, of course, is not to provoke misfortune and recklessly challenge that Hou Changjun, as the gap in realms is just too significant; all your schemes would be useless."

Chen Ping'an exited the prison, saying, "The peak of the Martial Husband realm, achieving Golden Core? You make it sound easy. You don’t know my current situation and plans, do you?"

The Outer Heavenly Demon trailed behind cheerfully, repeatedly clenching its fists, its arms raising higher than its head, shouting, "The old ancestor handles matters, regardless of size, with ease! A thousand-pound task, as light as a feather; timeless woes, like a drizzle; the old ancestor can turn clouds and rain with a wave of the hand…"

In retaliation, Chen Ping'an struck the Outer Heavenly Demon with a punch, causing it to shatter into pieces. After reforming in place, it hung its head, appearing listless, no longer a nuisance.

Being a loyal minister who refuses to be trusted is as bad as being a scheming flatterer who gets beaten. Truly, the hearts of the heavens are hard to read, accompanying a lord is akin to accompanying a tiger.

Chen Ping'an walked toward the pavilion below the prison.

The five Yuan Ying demon sword cultivators, led by Huang He, followed the general approach that Shuangjiang had outlined. The only goal was to take advantage of the time and place to surpass their opponents. In doing so, it certainly wouldn’t be a pure duel among sword cultivators, but it wouldn’t be considered anything less than fair either. Huang He and the others, as sword cultivators, also had their own secret techniques and hidden skills. Chen Ping'an’s greatest reliance was still the life-bound technique of the caged bird, a small world that leveled the playing field, while both sides were at half a realm. Additionally, he had the might of a martial artist from the Outer Realm as a backup.

According to Shuangjiang, as long as Chen Ping'an eventually ascended to the Yu Pu realm and nurtured the caged bird properly, the future "mutual rise and fall" would mean that they would each be at a different level—if one falls, the other rises. That would truly be the grand demeanor of a sword immortal, breaking through realms and slaying foes as easily as picking up coins off the ground.

However, these were all unattainable distant dreams, for now, they could only be wished for, a moment of happiness stolen.

Upon arriving at the pavilion, Chen Ping'an sat cross-legged, placing the narrow knife "Zhan Kan" across his knees. He began to breathe and meditate, tempering the remaining martial luck while simultaneously contemplating the business deal with Shuangjiang, multitasking with his cultivation.

After entering the Cave Dwelling realm, no matter how much Shuangjiang, who had ascended, didn’t take it seriously, for Chen Ping'an himself, accustomed to the ups and downs of the lower five realms, returning to cultivate as a middle five realms immortal felt entirely different.

As he breathed steadily, a white mist enveloped Chen Ping'an's face, the essence of spiritual energy swirling like delicate white serpents, hanging down from steep cliffs.

Especially at the center of his brow, a grain of inherent spiritual light flickered between brightness and darkness.

At the same time, the area around his eyes flowed with a faint golden hue, creating a pair of eyes that resembled two chambers, with two bright lights illuminating the entrance’s bamboo curtain.

This was the "Earthly Immortal, the Path of Enlightenment" that cultivators in the lower realms dreamed of.

Having fought five rounds with the Yuan Ying sword cultivators, whether it was honing his martial path, forcibly forging martial luck into the foundation of his bones, or checking for flaws through his injuries, he could be said to have gained immensely.

Shuangjiang adhered strictly to the rules, not stepping a single foot into the pavilion, like a wandering soul drifting outside.

Chen Ping'an's agreement with the Outer Heavenly Demon for a grain of Gu Yu money was also nearing its end.

A grain of Gu Yu money was divided into ten pieces of Xiao Shu money, all of which were payment for Shuangjiang’s life.

After gifting the execution weapon from the ancient Dragon-Slaying Platform, the narrow knife "Zhan Kan," Shuangjiang received the first piece of Xiao Shu money, marking a good start.

The inscription "This Heart of Spirit" could help Chen Ping'an sit in meditation and direct his energy more quickly and deeply, resembling the effect of a cultivator's meditation on an immortal's mat or lighting incense in a cave dwelling. Although it belonged to the method of "dripping water penetrating stone," it was not to be underestimated. Lower five realm cultivators, drawing energy from heaven and earth, were like cupping water with their hands, extremely difficult. Once they reached the middle five realm, it was as if they had a bucket to draw from a deep well, making the process much faster.

Chen Ping'an not only obtained a precious sword capable of suppressing the likes of a flood dragon but also a lasting benefit for his future path of cultivation—a significant profit.

For the second piece of Xiao Shu money, Chen Ping'an had Shuangjiang elaborate on the cultivation techniques for the Cave Dwelling realm, Observing Sea, and Dragon Gate realms, and all the combinations for refining life-bound items, both large and small.

Chen Ping'an decided to reach the Cave Dwelling realm within the prison. At that time, spiritual energy would flood into the small world, as Shuangjiang had assured him, this opportunity was once in a lifetime. By taking this chance to explore, he could help locate the ten mountains of the Crown Prince that had already opened their life-bound acupoints, successfully obtaining the third piece of Xiao Shu money.

While teaching, Shuangjiang, using her own abilities, managed to strike an additional business deal. She mentioned that the life-bound banner of the sword immortal needed to be erected at the peak of the mountain shrine using secret methods. At the time, she hadn’t gone into detail, so Chen Ping'an naturally took the bait. The Outer Heavenly Demon earned money while the Hidden Official, as a Cave Dwelling realm cultivator, gained an additional cultivation technique, adding icing on the cake.

Additionally, there was the imitation Baiyu Jing treasure pagoda, detailing how to open up new acupoints in the Observing Sea realm after refining it into a life-bound item. This could serve as an important auxiliary life-bound item, one that could absorb the essence of heaven and earth. The five elemental life-bound items naturally birthed within a person's small world could be refined here in the "Baiyu Jing," making it twice as effective, nurturing five life-bound items simultaneously. This was Shuangjiang’s timely assistance.

Moreover, she shared how to add the finishing touch to the water palace mural. The three secret techniques imparted to the Hidden Official by Shuangjiang cost Chen Ping'an only one piece of Xiao Shu money.

At this point, Shuangjiang had already secured four pieces of Xiao Shu money.

The two short swords that Shuangjiang spoke of casually, mentioning "Carving the Boat in Years Gone By," were intentionally vague. She did not wish to reveal their true roots. These two swords were inscribed with the characters "Dew" and "Lake," respectively. The former "Dew" sword had already been placed in Chen Ping'an’s sword nurturing gourd, so it didn't count as a transaction. However, the "Lake" sword, which Shuangjiang claimed would be a match for the Hidden Official, was priced at one piece of Xiao Shu money, which Chen Ping'an agreed to.

Unbeknownst to them, the Outer Heavenly Demon had already earned five pieces of Xiao Shu money.

Once Chen Ping'an reached the Dragon Gate realm, he could begin refining the two ancient relic swords into two water palace "dragon pools" for flood dragons. As for the water element flood dragon originally condensed from water dan, it would be refined into a water element black pearl. In the future, as his cultivation progressed, the thicker the water element became, the higher the grade of that black pearl.

The first piece of "Dew" sword would be given for free, while the benefits of the "Lake" sword's refinement, along with the sword immortal's banner and the imitation Baiyu Jing, were essentially the Outer Heavenly Demon fishing for profit, giving half the bait while keeping the other half.

Chen Ping'an didn’t mind Shuangjiang’s business tactics; after all, it was a fair transaction, not an act of coercion.

Furthermore, Shuangjiang had successively completed transactions with the materials from her true and false heavenly immortal cave attire, the two Qing Snakes hanging from her ears, as well as the entire sum of gold and fragments of her golden body that she split with "Longevity Dao Friend," resulting in four pieces of Xiao Shu money.

Only one piece of Xiao Shu money remained.

With a complete grain of Gu Yu money, as per their agreement, the Outer Heavenly Demon Shuangjiang could immediately leave the prison, gaining a boundless freedom. Moreover, once it departed, neither Chen Ping'an nor Chen Qingdu could target it again. As long as it did not follow the demon clan into the vast world of righteousness to harm any sword cultivators of the Sword Qi Great Wall, it could choose to become a ruler in the wilderness or hide in the vast world of righteousness, supporting puppets and establishing its own sect.

During this time, Shuangjiang had expressed willingness to defer one piece of snowflake money to buy a little story from Chen Ping'an.

In the end, Chen Ping'an quickly used a piece of snowflake money to exchange for the true material of the Five Thunder Seal from Shuangjiang.

Suddenly, Shuangjiang said, "I initially thought that insignificant snowflake money would become the decisive factor in our transaction. I didn’t expect you would so quickly alleviate my doubts."

Once Shuangjiang had secured nine pieces of Xiao Shu money, along with various scattered snowflake coins, even if they were just one snowflake coin short of a grain of Gu Yu money, the transaction still wouldn’t be completed.

The awkwardness for Shuangjiang, the Outer Heavenly Demon, lay in the fact that being short of one piece of Xiao Shu money was deadlock; even if it was just one snowflake coin short, it still meant the same.

Chen Ping'an remained with his eyes closed, frankly stating, "I had thought about making some moves with that snowflake coin at first, but then I changed my mind."

Shuangjiang halted, a worried expression on her face. "You’re not planning to withhold the last piece of Xiao Shu money, are you? Hidden Official, don’t do this; it’s too damaging to your reputation."

Chen Ping'an opened his eyes, shaking his head. "Of course not. You can live because of our first transaction involving the grain of Gu Yu money."

Shuangjiang nodded gently, puzzled. "I know this, but I’ve always found it hard to believe."

Chen Ping'an asked, "Do you really want to see Shuangjiang again? For an Outer Heavenly Demon who has gained pure freedom, is there really a need for such an obsession?"

Silence fell between them as Chen Ping'an continued, "You’re no longer anything akin to a celestial couple. Besides, with your cultivation and state of mind, when would you not be by the side of that great cultivator Shuangjiang, inseparable?"

For Shuangjiang, her heart demon was the woman he loved.

It should have been a connection of fate that Shuangjiang found after ascending to the upper five realms, only to become manifest when she ascended to the ascension realm. It was even possible that it happened when she attempted to reach the lost realms. This Outer Heavenly Demon truly came into being, yet Shuangjiang had never been able to completely eradicate this heart demon. Ultimately, they were worlds apart. It was likely that Shuangjiang had used some profound celestial method, merely exiling the heart demon without truly subduing or refining it. However, these were all mere conjectures without roots. The truth remained a mystery that only time could reveal, unless Chen Ping'an were to venture into the Qingming world, where he might see the real "Shuangjiang."

The Outer Heavenly Demon narrowed its eyes, asking, "How did you guess? Was it the embroidered handkerchief from that girl that revealed my origins, or was it when you touched my head, my instincts dodging?"

Chen Ping'an countered, "What’s there to guess? Wasn’t it you who wanted me to know the truth intentionally?"

The white-haired boyish-looking Outer Heavenly Demon smiled brightly, floating in the air, clapping lightly, genuinely praising, "Well done, Hidden Official. You truly never disappoint, Chen Ping'an."

Chen Ping'an said, "With the last piece of Xiao Shu money, let’s make a hundred-year agreement. Before we meet again, you will help me protect someone in secret."

The white-haired boy lightly flicked the green snake by his ear, saying, "In the Fifth World, only cultivators below the upper five realms are allowed to enter. I can’t go against Confucian rules. With intentions but no power, this task is hard for me. Chen Ping'an, aren’t you being unreasonable, deliberately making this difficult for me?"

Chen Ping'an shook his head. "My teacher is over there. I believe the Confucian sage guarding the pass will ultimately turn a blind eye. You only have one opportunity to act. After that, at most the Confucian sage will drive you out of the realm. At that time, you will follow my teacher’s escape plan, whether it’s returning to the vast world of righteousness, settling at Falling Ruins Mountain, or being imprisoned in the Lin of Meritorious Deeds. I will come to find you, no matter what the cost. I will honor my promise and restore your freedom. If you do not take action, we will meet in the Fifth World."

The white-haired boy asked, "What if…?"

Chen Ping'an replied solemnly, "What if I cannot keep my promise to find you? Regardless, after a hundred years, you will still gain your freedom."

The white-haired boy began to wander around the pavilion, seemingly weighing the pros and cons.

He began to discuss details with the young Hidden Official: "Scholars value face. If I were to hide this blatantly within a certain sword cultivator's soul, it wouldn’t really be hidden. Even if your teacher helps smooth things over, it wouldn’t be appropriate, would it? If Niangxin could enter the Fifth World, her soul must be deep enough, but she is in the Yu Pu realm and cannot go. This cannot be blamed on me. That great demon in the Capture and Release Pavilion—first, its expertise is specialized, and secondly, it can hide in the depths of a golden core sword cultivator’s mind, successfully fooling all the sword immortals. Obviously, this isn’t something that can be accomplished overnight. If you were to give me three to five years of time, I’d have a good chance of finding a golden core cultivator to occupy and take over."

Chen Ping'an said, "I will help you find a place to hide."

The white-haired boy sighed, "Hidden Official, your calculations are flawless. No matter how many words I have in my heart, when it comes to my lips, I find myself speechless."

Chen Ping'an stood up, reattaching Zhan Kan to his waist. "If you agree to this, I would appreciate it if you refrain from doing anything unnecessary in that brand new world. Don’t try anything 'just to see what happens.' Otherwise, you’ll be burning incense daily, praying for my death at the Sword Qi Great Wall."

Chen Ping'an chuckled, squinting his eyes, "In the past, I never liked to threaten anyone before a fight. Today, I’m making an exception for you, so cherish it."

The white-haired boy no longer wore a playful expression; he was now solemn and respectful, bowing deeply, "I shall comply with the old ancestor’s decree. From now on, a grain of Gu Yu money will count as a completed transaction."

Chen Ping'an leaned back, his hands resting behind his head, saying, "I’ll first test the depth of Meng Po and Qingqiu’s abilities. If I find myself helpless against them, I will then need to trouble you to step in with your own methods."

Chen Ping'an closed his eyes, stating, "Perhaps you intentionally led me to believe that the girl was the heart demon born from your affection. In reality, it was all just a ruse. It doesn’t matter; you win, and I haven’t lost anything."

The white-haired boy’s expression turned sorrowful, "Heroes live unfree; seeing you, the old ancestor, in such a hero's plight truly tugs at the heartstrings."

Chen Ping'an casually drew his sword, slashing through the air without so much as a glance at the Outer Heavenly Demon, who quickly reformed and hopped over to the pavilion, giving a thumbs-up repeatedly, "Not every hero can avert disaster; even a hero can be a calamity for the world, old ancestor… Oh, what a great sword technique!"

Niangxin sat on the distant steps, watching as the Outer Heavenly Demon and the azure-clad guest from the pavilion were likely to part ways, feeling a twinge of reluctance.

As a seamstress, she had never experienced such bustling activity on her path of cultivation, yet it felt so stable, free from the burdens of unforeseen plots from the mountains, and she had never been looked at as if she were a ghost.

The three of them walked down a desolate street. Li Cai wore a snow-white robe, a delicate white sword named "Frost Flood Dragon" hanging from her waist—its sheath now broken into two.

Alongside this female sect leader of the Floating Sea Sword Sect were the young man Chen Li and the girl Gao Youqing, both following Li Cai to Bei Ju Lu Zhou to become her direct disciples.

Li Cai believed she lacked the heroic flair of that Lu Zhi, her appearance having returned to how it was before. The scars on her cheeks were not very noticeable, yet her complexion was pale, indicating that she had not fully healed from her severe injuries. The real hidden danger lay in her life-bound flying sword, which had suffered significant damage. It was likely that she wouldn’t be able to hope for ascension to the Immortal realm in this lifetime. However, Li Cai didn’t mind; a woman with high cultivation faced difficulties in getting married, no matter how good her temper was.

This female sword immortal had been constantly battling since arriving at the Sword Qi Great Wall, always at the forefront. In the past few years, there had been many rules during the summer palace visits, and the Hidden Official’s messages via flying swords were the most annoying, imposing heavier restrictions on sword immortals. Among all the sword cultivators, it was certainly her, Li Cai, who insulted the young Hidden Official the most, far exceeding that of local sword cultivators.

After being severely injured and retreating from the city wall, she had relinquished all her war merits, only asking the Sword Qi Great Wall for a sword from the sword shop and a robe from the clothing shop.

There was a dear friend, the Great Xianjun Li Yu; they had once agreed to go to the Sword Qi Great Wall together to slay demons.

Upon reaching the tavern, Li Cai perused the "No Business" signs until she finally pulled down a "No Business" sign from the wall, grasping it tightly in her hand.

Not in a hurry to return to Bei Ju Lu Zhou, she intended to travel to Nan Po Sha Zhou for a bit, such as visiting the mountaintop of the sword immortal Yuan Qingshu.

Li Cai carried a heavily damaged sword nurturing gourd, a relic of Yuan Qingshu, which she should return to his sect.

Years ago, atop the city wall, Yuan Qingshu had once joked with local sword immortals Gao Kui, filling the sword nurturing gourd with wine and pairing it with the name of a great demon, making for an endless delight.

Yet both of them had died.

Li Cai turned to see two small heads peeking from the tavern’s entrance and smiled, "Tell the second shopkeeper that this 'No Business' sign has been taken by Li Cai."

Feng Kangle chuckled, "What does it matter? Just take it. A girl as pretty as you, if the second shopkeeper sees you, he wouldn’t dare say a word."

It was fine to go to another shop to buy wine, but causing a ruckus would disgrace their own tavern.

Tao Ban had a good memory, recalling all the customers who came to buy and drink in the tavern. "Sister Li, why hasn’t the second shopkeeper shown his face? Did he offend a lady again, making himself look all fancy while secretly slaying demons?"

Li Cai burst into laughter, "Sister Li? Did the second shopkeeper teach you that?"

Tao Ban nodded.

Feng Kangle complained, "You’re being so stupid; it’s not sincere at all."

Li Cai restrained her laughter, saying, "Bring me a pot each of every type of liquor; I’m taking them to Nan Po Sha Zhou."

Gao Youqing was etching words onto the "No Business" sign with her flying sword, while Chen Li raised an eyebrow, "What’s so good about that Pang Yuanji?"

Gao Youqing turned around, hiding the "No Business" sign, and retorted angrily, "You don’t get a say!"

Li Cai stood at the threshold of the tavern, gazing at the city wall.

She had come here to wield her sword freely, only to find her skills were far from sufficient, ultimately owing a tremendous debt of gratitude to that Yao Sword Immortal. The key was how she would repay it in the future.

The young boy looked dispirited, "Master, am I going to be a disciple of the Floating Sea Sword Sect from now on?"

Li Cai replied, "Then learn from this second shopkeeper. 'In the Vast World of Righteousness, Hidden Official Chen Ping'an. At the Sword Qi Great Wall, Floating Sea Sword Lake Chen Li. They do not interfere with each other. Hometown always comes first, while cultivation comes second, not forgetting one's roots.'"

The boy nodded; it was a plan.

Li Cai ultimately took the young boy and girl away from the Sword Qi Great Wall.

For the time being, there were no cross-province ferryboats docking at the Hanging Mountain toward Bei Ju Lu Zhou, so they casually found an immortal’s inn to stay in.

Li Cai drank alone.

Li Tui Mi, Tao Wen, Zhou Cheng, Nalan Ye Xing, Gao Kui, Yao Chong Dao, Dong San Geng…

There were so many young sword cultivators, many of whom were around the same age as Chen Li and Gao Youqing.

In the future, there would only be more.

Li Cai, with her drunken gaze, leaned against the window, thinking, "Just let this pathetic Jade Pu realm die."

Gao Youqing was staying next door, still adapting to the vastly different environment between the Hanging Mountain and the Sword Qi Great Wall. The spiritual energy and sword energy were worlds apart.

Chen Li was carefree, weighing his purse at a shop in the inn that specialized in selling treasures from the mountain. Since the entire Lingzhi Zhai had relocated, they had cleared out their inventory, selling many low-tier miscellaneous spiritual artifacts for cheap to the various factions in the Hanging Mountain, and this inn was one of them. Thus, the treasures here were limited, yet at first glance, they seemed to be a dazzling array of goods.

Observing from afar, Li Cai frowned at Chen Li’s sword intent, her killing intent surging as she dashed away.

Li Cai reached out to grab the boy’s life-bound flying sword, blood flowing from her palm, dripping to the ground, entirely unaware, as she said to Chen Li, "So many sword cultivators have died; it's not meant for you to come to the Vast World of Righteousness to die. If you truly wish to die, wait until you become a sword immortal before saying so. Killing an Observing Sea realm sword cultivator? Who would remember who you were? If you continue to be so impatient, you might as well become a wild cultivator in the mountains; you'd definitely die quickly. Otherwise, in the future, during your cultivation, you’d be the first to be killed, and I’d be left half-dead from anger, without knowing how to avenge you."

The individual targeted by Chen Li's flying sword was a flustered tavern keeper, who, upon seeing Li Cai, bowed deeply in apology, rambling on about many reasons: being blind to the situation, not deserving of death, and all that. Of course, it wasn’t a matter of beating and killing; in the end, it was Chen Li’s unstable sword intent, filled with murderous intent. Though he had already left the battlefield, his sword intent still resonated there.

This was a good thing, but if Li Cai continued to disregard it, then even if Chen Li made it to Bei Ju Lu Zhou, as soon as he descended the mountain to roam, he would die.

Li Cai opened her hand, and the young boy immediately retracted his flying sword.

Chen Li said apologetically, "I have no complaints against Master, nor against Bei Ju Lu Zhou."

Li Cai laughed, "Master doesn’t care about these things; just focus on whether you practice the sword well, and whether the Floating Sea Sword Lake can truly produce a Sword Immortal."

Chen Li sincerely replied, "Reaching sword immortal status within a hundred years is still somewhat challenging."

Li Cai clapped the boy on the shoulder, wiping the blood from her palm, "You’re a big man, show a bit of spirit! I, Li Cai, have direct disciples, even if you’re just a middle five realms sword cultivator. When you speak to others, especially when it comes to fighting, you must carry the air of an upper five realms sword immortal!"

Hearing the terms "Hundred-Year Sword Immortal" and "Centennial Sword Immortal," the tavern keeper's eyelids twitched, regretting it deeply as he hurriedly thought of ways to remedy the situation.

Li Cai and the boy exchanged heartfelt words, and the boy reluctantly "overpaid" for a spiritual artifact that had caught his eye.

As they returned to their lodgings, Li Cai asked him in a low voice, "Remember that fellow? Find a way to get back at him in the future."

Chen Li smiled broadly and nodded vigorously.

Li Cai knocked on Gao Youqing’s door, grabbing the girl’s cheek and twisting it, "Chen Li needs to hold back a bit. Gao Youqing, what’s wrong with you? Are you too timid and afraid of trouble? When Chen Li pulls out his sword, Master will stop him, but in his heart, he will be pleased. You, on the other hand, seem to enjoy watching from afar, without any thought of joining the fray? That makes Master very unhappy!"

Gao Youqing, having her cheek twisted, timidly said, "Master, my brother told me to endure once I arrived in the Vast World of Righteousness and absolutely not stir up trouble."

Li Cai scoffed, "It’s no wonder Gao Ye Hou is still a pitiful Yuan Ying."

Gao Youqing immediately teared up. 

Not only did she miss her brother, who had been her companion since childhood, but she also worried that their separation was not as simple as a mere parting; it was a quiet death.

Li Cai immediately released her grip, speaking softly, "Enough, enough. Endure if you must, but Master can teach you both a clever little trick. If you’re being bullied, bear with it, but if it’s a fellow disciple being bullied, then you can chop him to bits! Kill who needs to be killed, but don’t go around hacking indiscriminately. Just leave them half-dead; our Floating Sea Sword Lake still has some money, we can afford the medical bills! This way, you and Chen Li will have endured what you needed to endure and vented your anger. If it comes down to a real fight, just return home and call for Master to step in!"

At first, the young man and woman found it amusing, but upon hearing "return home," they fell silent, their spirits dampened.

Li Cai sighed lightly, waved her hand, and went to drink alone, leaving her disciples with the command, "Go practice your swords."

The old deaf man finally returned to the prison. You Yu and Chang Ming followed the elder, visiting the pavilion for the first time. 

The prison where Meng Po resided was already empty.

The old deaf man arrived at the stairs, glancing at the young Hidden Official within the pavilion, clad in an unfamiliar robe so large that its sleeves dragged on the ground.

Chen Ping'an seemed to be in a trance, completely unaware of the old deaf man’s arrival.

The old deaf man reached out, grabbing the jade hairpin that Chen Ping'an had tucked into his hair, bringing it to himself, and said solemnly, "The Master Sword Immortal needs to borrow this item for a short while and will return it to the Hidden Official soon."

Chen Ping'an remained unfazed.

The old deaf man glanced down at Niangxin, carefully tucking the jade hairpin into his sleeve. He didn’t trust the Outer Heavenly Demon, but he found this stubborn girl to be more reliable.

Noticing the old deaf man's scrutinizing gaze, Niangxin spoke up, "It’s fine, he asked for it; it has nothing to do with Wu Shuangjiang."

The woman who manifested from golden coins furrowed her brow slightly.

Shuangjiang smiled brightly, "Longevity Dao Friend, in worldly business, how can one take all the advantages? One must return nine for every ten taken; that is the principle. You should learn a thing or two from my old ancestor."

The woman nodded lightly.

You Yu, for some unknown reason, felt a little intimidated by the sight of the young Hidden Official at that moment.

The old deaf man hurriedly left, disappearing from the prison.

The boy and the woman ascended the stairs together.

Shuangjiang followed behind, asking, "Longevity Dao Friend, shall we continue to scour the land for treasures?"

The woman replied, "I’ve been waiting for this."

Gao Kui's final sword strike questioned the Sword Asking Founder, Dragon Lord.

After receiving the sword, Dragon Lord personally executed the last sword immortal of the lineage.

From a distance, in a gray long robe, the skeletal figure of Bai Ying sat on the throne, watching this scene unfold, feeling that the minds of these sword cultivators were indeed increasingly baffling.

**(End of Chapter)**
